# 如果神话传说都是真的，世界会变成什么样子？
- 点赞数：273392
- 更新时间：2023年06月28日11时34分16秒
- 回答url：https://www.zhihu.com/question/36260262/answer/67686600
<body>
 <p>1</p>
 <p>淅淅沥沥的小雨打在屋檐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅起一片片水雾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>云压得极低<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>让人喘不上气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是雷震子与索尔的第六次斗法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他吃了大亏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>羽毛被火燎掉了一半<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>露出鲜红的肉翼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>空气中弥漫着浓郁的蛋白质烧焦气味<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>如马尔克斯在<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>百年孤独<span class=" fw-cl "><span>》</span></span>里形容的一般<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雷震子买了一张永久车票<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>登上了一列永无终点的火车<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是必死的征途<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雷震子选择加入东方仙人联盟的那一刻就已经料到了结局<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>可他不能后退哪怕一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>因为身后有他的亲友<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有他的祖国<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还有 14 亿毫无能力的普通人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他艰难地爬起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手里抓着已经残破不堪的黄金棍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用尽全力挥向索尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>何苦呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>索尔叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>因为我的双膝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只跪给父母<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>2</p>
 <p>公元 2015 年 11 月 7 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>梵蒂冈教廷联合世界树密会发表声明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>要求全部人类立即停止一切科学研究<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>放弃对神之秘宝的探索<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>避免毁灭性打击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>世界一片哗然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>《</span></span>纽约时报<span class=" fw-cl "><span>》</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>《</span></span>英国太阳报<span class=" fw-cl "><span>》</span></span>等刊文<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>神棍的妄想症严重到必须送入医院强制治疗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>官方网站公开投票<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>70% 以上美国民众表示赞同<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>各国外交部均予以不理睬政策<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>次日凌晨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大不明生物袭击米国白宫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其夷为平地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>白宫护卫军队全军覆没<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伤亡人数过万<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后世称其<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>十一•八袭击<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>」</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>据目击者称<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>袭击者骑乘一匹十数米高的八足巨马<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手掌掷矛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每次出手必定毁灭目标<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>疑似北欧主神奥丁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>米国全面进入战争状态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进行了英勇的抵抗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但加入战争的神越来越多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>米军节节败退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几欲亡国<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>终于<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>米国动用了核武器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2015 年 12 月 25 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>10 万米军以生命为代价拖住几位神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>50 万吨级的原子弹在内华达州和亚利桑那州交界地带的黑峡引爆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>胡佛溃坝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>下游地区洪水泛滥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后世称之为<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>上帝之殇<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>」</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>森林之神维达<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>智天使加百列在此役中陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>教廷和金宫震怒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>对人类全面开战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>第三次世界大战就此拉开序幕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>战火烧遍了全球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>更多的神想要分一杯羹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>奥林匹斯山派使者觐见奥丁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>组成欧洲神祇联盟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2016 年 2 月 3 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>欧洲神祇联盟进军日国<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>日国本土神祇迎战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2016 年 2 月 7 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>日国发生 9.2 级地震<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>富士山爆发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>火之迦具土神在决斗中陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>八岐大蛇被斩五首<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>受天照营救落荒而逃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>日国沦陷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>此事一出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天下大震<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>李耳出面组织东方仙人联盟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>与欧洲各神祇对峙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进入冷战阶段<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>双方众神相互敌对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摩擦迅速升级<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2016 年 5 月 5 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雷震子决斗索尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>玉柱洞云中子大怒出山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一天之内手刃洛基<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>狄俄尼索斯等多位欧洲神祇为徒弟报仇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>至此<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双方再无回旋余地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大战一触即发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>3</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>C 组已就位<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请通报敌人位置<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>完毕<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>北偏东 34 度 12 分<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直线距离 2 千米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣殿骑士 102 人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带队天使乌里叶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无异常反应<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>完毕<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>天气有些阴冷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>秋风瑟瑟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杨戬的斗篷微微浮着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有一种飘逸的美<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>C 组只有两个人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再精确一点<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是一人一狗——杨戬和哮天犬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他们搭档了上千年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>早已经有了默契<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>侦察突袭的任务也做了不止一次<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>至今还未失手过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这次联盟派遣他俩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也是因为对方护送的东西确实至关重要<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬揉了揉哮天犬的头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>站起了身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他想起当年和孙悟空打的那一架<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那才叫爽快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不知道这 1800 多年后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>面对西洋神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>能不能再找回酣畅的感觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>杨戬很期待<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的三尖两刃刀已经很久没沾血了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>让我见见你们的本事吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬嘴角上扬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向敌人疾驰而去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他丝毫不掩饰的冲刺带起滚滚尘土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同一条青龙直插阵中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>乌里叶瞬间就进入了战斗状态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神情严肃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他能感觉到面前敌人的强大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便拥有智天使称号的自己应付起来也绝对不容易<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬持刀前刺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>暴戾的风在刀身打转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那一瞬间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是把空气都劈成了两半<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>乌里叶大惊失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>六翼挥动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向后躲避<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>同时用手中圣剑格挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>只一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乌里叶的剑就飞了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>杨戬哈哈大笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你这鸟人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>和泼猴相比差得太多了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>乌里叶不敌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两人斗了才不到 10 个回合<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哮天犬一口咬在乌里叶脚踝处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扯住了他的身体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>杨戬闪到乌里叶身后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>挟住他的翅膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大喝一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>撕了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>乌里叶痛苦地哀号<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杨戬把他踩在脚下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>迎着圣殿骑士们恐惧的目光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扭断了他的脖子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而后悠悠一叹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>寂寞啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哮天犬附和着汪了两声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>趾高气扬地站在主子身边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬掏出震动许久的对讲机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>按下了接听键<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>快逃啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嗯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>巨大的魔狼直扑杨戬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他嗅到那巨口中死亡与血腥的恶臭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第一次感受到了危险<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那是能轻易切断战神提尔手腕的利齿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是能吞噬日月的死神獠牙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>汪呜——<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>）</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哮天犬跃起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拦在主人身前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是眨眼间就隐没于芬里厄的嘴中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哮天<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬红了眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>三尖两刃刀由芬里厄的喉咙刺进心脏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狼血染红了白甲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>灌江口相遇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>三渡于草莽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬剖开了芬里厄的肚子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼泪止不住地滴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哮天犬把眼睛睁开一点缝隙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸出舌头舔掉杨戬的泪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摇了摇尾巴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再也不动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>对讲机里传出撤退的命令<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杨戬一脚将其踩碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仰天长啸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>第三只眼霍然圆瞪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一丝阴云掩盖了日光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>要流血了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2016 年 10 月 7 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杨戬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>哮天犬遭遇陷阱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩杀智天使乌里叶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后与中庭之蛇耶梦加德<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>魔狼芬里厄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>冥界女王海拉三兄妹同归于尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>4</p>
 <p>相比各路神仙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猴子总是无忧无虑的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>今天喝点小酒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>明天吃点水果<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着手下一帮小弟开开心心地在花果山上嬉游<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这就是孙悟空最大的快乐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>神间的大战没波及大雷音寺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空倒也乐得清闲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>做一个闲散佛陀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阳光铺在水帘之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>透点波光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照亮了孙悟空的面庞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空斟了杯酒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把酒洒在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>酒滴被穿堂风卷着散在空气里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>映出一道彩虹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>顿了一会儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又另斟了一杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>语带悲伤道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>真君啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天庭里三清四御纵然法力无边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺老孙也不曾服气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>唯独你不同<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哪想百年未见<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你却落得个神魂俱灭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>唉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这樽仙酿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺老孙先干为敬了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空将杯中的酒一饮而尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>久久不语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>报告大王<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>外面有个肥头大耳的人说要见你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>几只小猴毛手毛脚地窜进水帘洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲着孙悟空叫道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空收起悲戚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哈哈笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>孩儿们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把他给我押上来<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>几只小猴闻令告退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只等了片刻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便带了一胖子上殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那胖子被捆得结结实实<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不断地挣扎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>破口大骂道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你这该死的弼马温<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>上千年过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>连点花样都不换<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空走上前去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>打量胖子一番道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我当是谁呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>原来是八戒啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>什么风把你吹到我这小山头了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>弼马温<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你先把你猪爷爷放下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>我有急事和你说<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空转身回到自己座位上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拿起个桃子咬了一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摆了摆手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>含糊不清地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>给这呆子掌嘴<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哎哎哎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猴哥儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你在那诸天神佛里都是排得上号的人物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怎好与俺老猪这样不识眼色的小人物计较<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>八戒急忙讨饶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空听了好笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吩咐猴子们给猪八戒松绑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>询问他来意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大事不好啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大师兄<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>八戒急切地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>俺和沙师弟陪师父去那金宫说和劝善<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>本想着平稳事态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪想那些小神野蛮得很<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两句不和就要动手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我拼尽一身法力才闯了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可沙师弟却被打成重伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>师父也被擒住了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空脸色越来越阴沉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后一拳砸下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>桌子瞬间化为齑粉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>酒杯碎了一地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>蠢货<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>孙悟空气得牙根痒痒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>师父要是出了什么事情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我扒了你这一身猪皮<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒唯唯诺诺的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不敢搭话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空站直身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神情严肃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>召来了全部猴子猴孙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>孩儿们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺老孙寄情山水千年的自由全是俺师父给的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>现在师父有难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺就算是拼上这条薄命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也必须要帮<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>孙悟空中气十足道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>尔等就在花果山好生候着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照顾好这呆子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>待俺杀上那甚么劳什子金宫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>救出师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再回来给孩儿们奖赏<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空语毕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>窜了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踏上筋斗云<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几个跟斗风驰电掣便杀向金宫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>欺人太甚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>实在是欺人太甚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>今天就要让这群狗屁伪神知道孙爷爷的厉害<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>头配凤翅紫金冠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身被锁子黄金甲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>足踏藕丝步云履<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手擎如意金箍棒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空逆风而行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒吼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将棍子甩了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>轰——!<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>英灵殿的正门被孙悟空一棍击破<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奥丁骇然抬头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>露出了难以置信的神色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>吃俺老孙一棒<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>铁棒飞到空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>愈变愈大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直到二人环抱粗细<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒啸横扫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>斯雷普尼尔挡在奥丁面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被金箍棒砸个正着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>骏马一声悲嘶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不断喷吐的雷云闪电消散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>八只巨足尽数折断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奥丁金色的双眸中燃烧起怒火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手紧紧握住 永恒之枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>世界树枝制成的枪柄泛起熔金般的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>昆古尼尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>永恒之枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>在阿萨神族和华纳神族开战时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就是由奥丁拿着这把神枪投出第一击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它的能力极致单纯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却暴力无比<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那就是——必杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>昆古尼尔所指向的任何敌人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都会被刺穿胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>奥丁愤怒地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他举起昆古尼尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奋力掷出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耀目的光芒如闪电般划破天空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>星辰黯淡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>日月失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就连时间都在瞬间停止<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>除了孙悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>如意金箍棒缩小到正和手的大小<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空抬起手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>毫无二心地将金箍棒指向身前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同能预知昆古尼尔的轨迹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>破<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>光芒炸碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>奥丁喷出金色的血液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无力地坐在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他艰难地开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>为什么……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>超脱三界外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不在五行中<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空缓缓说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而后拔下来一簇毫毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>撒在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>开始吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2016 年 10 月 24 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斗战胜佛孙悟空大闹英灵殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>击杀镇守者主神奥丁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>成功营救旃檀功德佛唐玄奘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>金身罗汉沙悟净此前护法身受重伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>次日于花果山陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>5</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我猛然惊醒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>握住了腰间的格洛克<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>周围没有天使<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有恶魔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也没有其他什么形形色色奇怪的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我长出一口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>擦了擦冷汗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我是一个普通人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不会仙术<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不会异能<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在神与神的夹缝中苟活<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尽管 5 年前我还不相信有神这种东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这个世界对我们普通人其实很不友好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>或许以前是友好的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但现在我只能感受到满满的恶意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灼得我浑身疼痛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就在 5 年前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我还是个中二的少年的时候<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第三次世界大战爆发了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>同学死了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>学校被毁成一片废墟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>亲人被突如其来的袭击冲散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的机会来了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是我成为屠龙骑士的最好机会<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我将仗剑天涯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>远方的公主等待着我的拯救<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>然后骑士来了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>砍了公主的头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一把火烧了我的家<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我这才知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>骑士不只是屠龙的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们有时也是普通人的刽子手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我的梦想随着滚滚升腾的浓烟一起消散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>时间会改变很多东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>于我来说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>热血凉了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我只是依靠手里的枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>机械地复仇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>担惊受怕地活着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我为什么还不死呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我也不知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>或许是怕疼吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我起身站直<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸了个懒腰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>关节嘎嘣嘎嘣地响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>天空还是布满阴云<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>核冬天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我嗤笑了一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>收拾好行装<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掩饰了自己过夜的痕迹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>端着枪上路<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>c17 呼叫总部<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请求弹药补充<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>完毕<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>距离你此刻位置直线距离 12 千米处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是华夏第七陆军基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你可以在那获得补给<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>路线已发送至你的个人 PDA<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>祝你好运<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>中士<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>对讲机中传出了冰冷的女声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我打开 PDA<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>调出路线图<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是条曲折的路线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>估计不会好走<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但我别无选择<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>生活磨平了我的棱角<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但却让我更加坚韧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这或许是唯一的好处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>4 小时后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我站在了基地门口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这里喧闹不堪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>所有人都在备战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我拽住一位士兵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向他询问情况<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>米迦勒要亲自带军攻打这里<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>大天使长米迦勒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我微微叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>同情地看了一眼这个即将不复存在的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身离去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>小九<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>有个声音脆生生地叫住了我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我回头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>惊喜地发现这个声音来自李秋沐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>曾经照顾过我的姐姐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那是 5 年前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她拉住了我的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把我从楼顶拉下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用一记耳光扇醒了我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>让我断了自杀的念头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那时候她说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不要被懦弱压倒啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>我一直谨记在心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>胖子笑眯眯地看着我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小猫还是一副不理人的模样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>顺子叼着烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲我挥挥手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我上去拥抱他们每个人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心中泛起了久违的温暖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我最终没有离开基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>当天夜里我喝了许多的酒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在 PDA 里加了联系人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>约定加入他们的团队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我们讲述了自己离别 4 年来的经历<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阵阵唏嘘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>呜——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>防空警报的声音响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我倏然起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脑袋狠狠地撞了一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着眼前的路虎方向盘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一阵迷茫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我甩了甩头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>宿醉的感觉告诉我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>昨天的一切都是真实发生的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>可是现在却只有我一个人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>防空警报还在继续<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我下了车<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>打开后备厢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>满满两大箱武器弹药<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还有近乎奢侈的汽油和食物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>充足得像是大战之前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我隐约意识到了什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我急忙掏出 PDA<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>找到李秋沐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>按下了通话键<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>时间一分一秒过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正当我抓心挠肝时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>终于通了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>对面杀声震天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>枪炮怒吼混成一片<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>李秋沐语气冷淡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>什么事<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沐姐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是米迦勒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大天使长<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你打不过他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是螳臂当车<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>她沉默了一会儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我已经决定了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我把所有的东西都给你了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>你要活着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不要被懦弱压倒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神也是能够被杀死的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你还有很多机会<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>我怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>小九<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你说真的会有天堂吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>沐姐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>别掺和了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们不行的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们是神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>小九<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你长大了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李秋沐发出一声轻笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后是机枪扫射的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我仿佛能看到她矫健的身影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她架着机枪杀死一个又一个圣殿骑士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>短发被灼热的空气吹得飞扬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>红色的十字架在米迦勒手中闪耀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在乌云中隐约透出的日光照射下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>炽天使的六翼舒展<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我仿佛听见肉体被切割的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>小猫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你听我说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你现在出城找我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们一起离开这儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们没必要去送死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是没有意义的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么能是没有意义的呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>小猫淡淡地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我们的亲人在战火中连尸骨都没能留下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们的朋友一个接着一个倒在眼前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们的土地上布满了异族人的军队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而现在我们终于可以用自己所拥有的东西去换点什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怎么能是没有意义的呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你怎么那么死心眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你付出自己的命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>米迦勒也不会掉一根羽毛<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>小猫说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那也无所谓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>胖子已经死了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他在我面前被斩断了四肢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他说你跑啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>和小九一起跑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小九是个好男孩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你是个好女孩<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我感受到了小猫无尽的悲痛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深入骨髓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那个一直笑眯眯的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那个始终挡在她面前的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那个曾经揉着她的头发的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在她的面前被砍掉了四肢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>让她逃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>杀了他们<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>我喃喃道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我会的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>小猫握着匕首<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>切开一个又一个敌人的喉咙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>骑士剑从她背后插入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又从胸口透出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>头绳滑脱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缎子般的秀发散开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>圣殿骑士眼神淡漠地看着她<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小猫咧开嘴笑了笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲骑士脸上吐了一口血痰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>她的头颅被斩了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我坐在驾驶位<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>愤怒地砸方向盘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼泪不争气地流<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>九哥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你那有烟吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>顺子问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>有<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你来找我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>顺子呵呵一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>点在我的坟前<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你们都是傻逼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你们以为自己遇到神上去送死很高尚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>都是蚍蜉撼大树<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>全是送死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我听到顺子点起一根烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他说是啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们都是去送死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可是除了送死我们还能做什么呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>我们在这世界上苟延残喘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>永远只是个蝼蚁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们就只剩下了拼命的权利<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>所以我要去死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我无言以对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>圣殿骑士的长剑闪烁着圣光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似乎要从顺子的灵魂中照出点什么阴暗的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>顺子掐灭了烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把手枪上了膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>指向圣殿骑士的脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>真丑啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我的胸口如同压了一块巨石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>沐秋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>胖子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>小猫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>顺子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们把生的希望给了我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>自己走向充斥着烈火的深渊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不要被懦弱压倒啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我启动车子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用尽全力转动方向盘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踩下了油门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>6</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>三太子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总部发来消息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>索尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>哈迪斯两大实力神祇正往这边行军<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咱们该撤退了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒用手指点着桌子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>再等等<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>土地公公<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我想见见索尔<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>土地神叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从帐篷里退了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒明白土地神的担忧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冥王哈迪斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>雷神索尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不知道有多少东方仙人倒在他们面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一旦和他们对上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以自己的能力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恐怕凶多吉少<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但他仍然想知道杀了雷震子的人究竟长什么样子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪怕明知风险<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒心中烦躁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>起身从帐篷中出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>天空中阴云密布<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直压着地平线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>戈壁滩边的小绿洲似乎都带上了墨迹的颜色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>风如刀子般贴着他的脸庞划过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扬起一道道沙土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>5 年来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双方都受了极大的损失<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>下层天兵天将陨落者不计其数<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哪吒不能理解西方众神的行为<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>为什么要杀戮呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>为什么不能共处呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>都已经有了无限的寿命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>为什么还要贪图更多的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>没人告诉哪吒他是为了什么而战斗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他只是机械地攻击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>防御<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>偶尔想起雷震子等故去的挚友<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便更坚定了自己的信念<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>三太子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咱们真的该撤退了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>危险系数太高<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总部那边催了许多次了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>土地神又一次走到哪吒身边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>焦急地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你们先走吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我再等等<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒面无表情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哎哟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的三太子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那索尔什么时候见不行啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>这次是真的危险<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咱们驻守的神将就只有您一人堪堪一战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>根本不可能挡住索尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>哈迪斯联手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留得青山在<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不怕没柴烧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您就听我一次<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>土地神絮絮叨叨说了一大堆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒不耐烦道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我命令你们现在收拾行装撤离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的问题我会自己和总部说<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>土地神还想再说什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却见哪吒摆摆手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只好告退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>很快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>驻守临时基地的众小神都收拾好行装<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一一与哪吒告别<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>土地神是最后一个走的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>三太子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小神承蒙李天王提携<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>当上这一官半职<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无以为谢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>儿时习得一招防护秘法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请让我为您加持<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>任由土地神用血在自己的手腕上刺下一道符印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>刺罢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>土地神深深地看了哪吒一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>旋身消失不见<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>风越来越大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>漫天的沙尘遮掩了视线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>本来没多少光线的营地显得更加阴森<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>混天绫在风中噼啪作响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哪吒如雕像般伫立在营地中央<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他合着双目<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不知道是养神还是思考<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>远方传来行军的人声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒睁开眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>影影绰绰的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看不清楚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但他知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是敌人来了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒微微俯身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把 PDA 放在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后踏上了风火轮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>几千里外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>土地神坐在自己的小庙里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>痛苦地捂着胸口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那上面焦黑一片<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似被闪电击中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>是替生符咒的效果<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>老人紧紧握住竹杖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>爽朗地笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角流下鲜红的血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一如混天绫的颜色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>哪吒刚和索尔对拼了一记<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>乾坤圈打碎了索尔半扇肋骨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的闪电也击穿了自己的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哪吒看了一眼手腕已经消失的符咒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这东西还真不错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>倒是可以推广一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒定下心神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手一翻甩出一块金砖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>索尔急忙抬起重锤格挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>巨大的金铁交击声后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两人同时退了一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是你杀了雷震子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>索尔一愣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没想到面前的人会问他这个问题<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的眼中闪过一丝怀念<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他是值得尊敬的对手<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒沉默了一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>激发了火枣的仙力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>三头六臂破体而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>火尖枪泛起金光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>与阴阳剑的青气纠缠在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绕着哪吒盘旋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是一瞬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>气势恢宏如斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我会杀了你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>索尔举起锤子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雷电四溢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>请便<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>两人同时弓身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如脱弦之箭般碰撞在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中兵器相触<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深蓝的电弧与红色长绫不断地碰触分离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似两条长身蛟龙共舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>七彩的电浆飞溅喷涌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一时间竟是天地失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒右脚一顿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身体绕着索尔转了个圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>混天绫顺势攀上索尔的右手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>控制了他的行动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哪吒四臂齐抬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阴阳剑与火尖枪就要插进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊——<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒发出了撕心裂肺的咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>五马分尸一样的痛苦使他瞬间大脑一片空白<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>三头地狱犬刻耳柏洛斯喷薄着恶臭气息的巨口咬住了哪吒的手臂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>疯狂地撕了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>蛇尾一甩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将哪吒抽飞出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>身上毒蛇化成的毛发喷吐着毒液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>落到地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乌头草蓬勃生长<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哈迪斯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>索尔转身怒视<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不要插手我的战斗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哈迪斯无所谓地耸了耸肩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脸上露出阴毒的笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>呵……呵……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒喘着粗气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从地上爬了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>断臂处血流滚滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>刻耳柏洛斯喷出一口黑气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲向哪吒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正当獠牙即将碰触哪吒的咽喉时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒突然收回了六臂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九龙烈火罩祭出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将地狱三头犬镇在其中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>烈焰贴上刻耳柏洛斯的皮毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>化为九条火龙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>滚滚龙吟与刻耳柏洛斯的悲嗥混合在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒一步踏出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>朵朵莲花在乌头草中绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哈迪斯变了脸色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>谨慎地举起双叉戟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>作出迎战的姿态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒双目清明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>松开了手里的兵器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>混天绫与乾坤圈化为一金一红两道光束<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲入云霄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在乌云中炸碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>积压已久的阴霾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>消散了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>阳光穿过乌云中央的大洞散射下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正打在哪吒身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绽放出万道霞光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>索尔突然有种朝拜的冲动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒仿佛能听到雷震子和杨戬等已故挚友的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他们说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>歇息吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>百朵莲开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2020 年 5 月 17 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒独自拦截敌军<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩杀三头地狱犬刻耳柏洛斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>冥王哈迪斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重创雷神索尔后化莲陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>陈塘关土地神因替身符咒共殒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>7</p>
 <p>匕首在阿努比斯的手中翻飞跳跃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他思索着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>久久才开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>阿普切先生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请允许我这么称呼您<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您怎么能让我们相信<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您是带着诚意来的呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>阿普切摸了摸自己的雪橇铃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用嘶哑的声音说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>库库尔坎会献出它的一枚血麟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阿努比斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你知道那意味着什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是伊扎姆纳大人的底线了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>库库尔坎的血麟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>阿努比斯的气息有些粗重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他和荷鲁斯对视一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都看到了对方眼里的惊喜与贪婪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>据说得到库库尔坎的血麟就可以提升神格的层次<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这几乎是每个神祇都梦寐以求的机缘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿努比斯压住心中的热切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刚要开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被空气中震动的能量惊得站了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>荷鲁斯冲他摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>安抚他坐下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拉威严的声音倏然响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我可以答应你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阿普切先生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但我还有一个要求<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>伟大的太阳神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您请说<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>阿普切尊敬地弯下自己的腰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这位的神力远不是他所能及的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他必须摆出一定的姿态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>同意撒旦的加入<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>拉的声音震慑人心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他会使我们的联军更加无往不摧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>阿普切微微沉吟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>如您所愿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>巨灵神整整两天没能睡个好觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他所在的基地是华夏最强的基地之一<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>除非是十二泰坦或是密米尔这样的强大存在袭击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>否则陷落的可能性近似为零<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>可他还是隐隐不安<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他在这儿只是一个小小的士官<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但他还是和托塔天王说了自己的预感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>天王派了顺风耳和千里眼侦察<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却是什么也没发现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>巨灵神点起一根香烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是他在人间发现的好东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>烟雾由他嘴中吐出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>盘旋而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>消散在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一丝阴云遮住了阳光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑色的碎片在空中凝结拼装<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一点点成型<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>狰狞的巨门拔地而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血腥之气扑面而来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那一瞬间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨灵神听到了无数冤死的魂灵痛苦的尖号<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>狗头人身的神灵轻轻地落在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨灵神甚至无法回忆起他出现的方式<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似乎他本来就该在那里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他左手擎着一柄宽刃镰刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手拿着一块黑曜石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲巨灵神作了个揖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>赞美你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>啊拉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向着你惊人的上升<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span></p>
 <p>你上升<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照耀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>令诸天向一旁滚动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>你是众神之王<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>万物之主<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span></p>
 <p>我们自你而来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>因你而成神圣<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他将黑曜石拍进了巨门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨门瞬间燃起了血色的烈焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>巨灵神瞪大了眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>香烟掉在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅起火花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>敌袭<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>一道光箭穿过巨灵神的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他张着嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声音被扼在喉咙里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓倒地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>身后三对黑翼的天使狂笑着从地狱之门中飞出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中握着十字长剑末日审判<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他舞了个剑花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>长啸道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>路西法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>晨星之子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向你们问好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>地狱之门一次次窜出火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越来越多的恶魔从里面钻出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>十只<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>百只<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>千只<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>万只<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>无数恶魔咆哮着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒吼着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>举起自己的武器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲向基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>踏平<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>踏平<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>杀戮一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>毁灭一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>李靖看着眼前的景象<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>紧紧攥住了自己的宝塔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他想起了千年前面对陈塘关大水时的无力感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>恶魔如潮水般涌来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>众仙纷纷祭出法宝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>逆锋而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>萨麦尔尖笑着剜出千里眼的眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>塞进嘴里咬碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液涂满了牙齿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>手中长枪挥舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刺穿一枚又一枚心脏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>吕洞宾下腰躲开亚巴顿的斧击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>单手撑地腾空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>折扇直插过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>亚巴顿后撤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正迎上铁拐李的重拳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>只一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拳气便打折了他的脊椎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>圣甲虫从泥土里钻出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>淹没了倒地的天兵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>惨叫声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>喊杀声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论恶魔还是仙人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都杀红了眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿努比斯挥动着死神镰刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>剧毒的黑烟缠上李靖的宝剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>李靖松开剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>祭出玲珑宝塔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将阿努比斯镇在下面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>撤啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>都撤啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李靖撕心裂肺地怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>红色的手指插入他的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻地掏出了心脏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>撒旦伸出舌头轻轻舔舐着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>火焰将心脏烧成灰烬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>李靖矗立不倒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>撒旦饶有兴致地看了他一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身离开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在地上留下一串烧焦的足印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2021 年 3 月 12 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第三方加入战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>恶魔联军袭击东西双方军队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使其伤亡惨重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>托塔李天王等众多仙人陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>天使军团除拉斐尔一人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全军覆没<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2021 年 4 月 7 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>十二泰坦参战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大战雨神恰克<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>死神阿普切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>灵宝道君出山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>上等神位者正式加入战斗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>8</p>
 <p>宙斯已经逃了三天三夜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他从来没这么窝囊过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以他的神力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即使是十二泰坦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也可以拼个平手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但是他却被一个老头儿打得连他妈都认不出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大部分伤是被那老头儿牵着的青色水牛踢的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这简直是耻辱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>宙斯恨不得自己把自己弄死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>小娃娃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们又见面了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我艹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>老头儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你骑的是火箭吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯大惊失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸手聚集起了雷霆怒火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轰向老头儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那老头儿随手一挥扁拐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把雷霆打散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>笑呵呵道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>娃娃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你这小闪电倒是有趣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>虽是兵器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却不能被我那金刚琢收了去<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯听了差点气得吐血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span>我无往不利的雷霆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在你嘴里变成了小闪电<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟然还说不错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有没有这么寒碜人的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯又甩出一道雷霆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>飞速逃亡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眨眼间便消失无踪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>老头儿伸手擒住雷霆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翻来覆去地瞧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脸上露出好奇的神色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>高加索山脉的罡风没日没夜地冲刷着岩石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>巨大的铁链哗啦作响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>与地上巨鹰的尸骨构成一片荒凉之景<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>伊阿佩托斯的儿子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尊贵的王<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的好朋友<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我遇到了最大的劫难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>渴求您的帮助<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>宙斯立在木屋门前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>低沉地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>门开了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>普罗米修斯把宙斯迎进屋内<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他倒了两杯酒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>放在桌上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>伟大的众神之父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>追袭您的人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>名曰太清太上老君<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他几乎是世界上最顶尖的神祇了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我不认为自己比您更有能力与他战斗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯摇晃着酒杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我需要您的智慧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>普罗米修斯笑了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>伟大的神父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您真的会听我的吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>曾经我跟您说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不要因为答应保护人类而提出苛刻的献祭条件<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您没收了人类的火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我把火种带给人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您却用一条永远也挣不断的铁链把我缚在这儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使我永远不能入睡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>疲惫的双膝不能弯曲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您在我起伏的胸脯上钉上金刚石的钉子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我忍受着饥饿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>风吹和日晒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>被巨鹰啄食肝脏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>难道我再一次劝您放弃对人类的讨伐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您就会听从我的吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不会<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>普罗米修斯爽朗地笑了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将麦酒一饮而尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>去找您的父亲吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他会助您在这条路上越走越远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尽管我并不看好这条路的前途<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哈哈哈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小娃娃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不要躲了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君的声音在木屋外响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯脸色铁青<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手心凝聚起滚滚惊雷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>普罗米修斯的手落在他的肩膀上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摇了摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯散了手中的雷霆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>疑惑地看向普罗米修斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您走吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伟大的众神之父<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>普罗米修斯淡淡地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>推开了木屋的门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>咦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怎么又有一个人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>小娃娃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你是做什么的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君惊奇道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>阻拦你的人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2021 年 5 月 12 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太清太上老君李耳斩杀普罗米修斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重伤宙斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2021 年 5 月 15 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>克洛诺斯与其子宙斯约定同盟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即日纠集十二泰坦进攻华夏陆军第七基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>遭通天教主摆诛仙阵坑杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>炽天使米迦勒陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>十二泰坦陨落四位<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>通天教主重伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>9 <em>Day One</em><span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>Hans Zimmer</p>
 <p>火焰从焦土中开放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凝成一朵朵曼珠沙华<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>炎热的空气烧灼着恶魔的皮肤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使其发出一声声痛苦的哀号<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>恶魔们无一不看着中央的身影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>难以移目<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>除了贝利尔以外都匍匐在他的脚下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那身影正跳一曲舞蹈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>暴戾与优雅合二为一<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>释放出惊人的气势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天的愤怒如恒河洪水般汹涌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着毁灭一切的意志席卷恶魔大军<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>贝利尔嘴中苦涩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他本来是领命带兵偷袭败退的十二泰坦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>结果却遇到了这个从未见过的家伙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他自称湿婆天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只凭舞蹈便使得数万的恶魔进退不得<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>随着湿婆天激昂的舞步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大地开始震动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>曼珠沙华浮在空中盘旋萦绕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>梵风蒸腾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恶魔开始自燃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>贝利尔一声怒嚎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>挣脱了束缚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他挥动四翼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直冲湿婆天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>要是再不做点什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一切就都玩完了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>贝利尔浑身的皮肤在梵风中摩擦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>火焰蹿了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他似彗星一般<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绽放出夺目的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天诧异地看了他一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力朝地上跺了一脚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>浑圆的冲击波拦住贝利尔冲刺的势头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>贝利尔绝望地呻吟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>曼珠沙华放射出金光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轰然爆破<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>烈焰吞没了恶魔军团<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>硝烟散尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>贝利尔趴在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>皮肤满是龟裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他能清楚地感到自己的内脏都被烤熟了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天优雅地踩着他走过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>足尖点碎了他衰弱的心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>木总理<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直升机已经准备好了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>您该走了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>木阳站在城楼之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俯视着下方已经面目全非的北平城<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的心在颤抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>请再让我和我的祖国待一会儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>浓烟不知道从哪个胡同升起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>现在的北平城到处都是火灾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>令人不禁想起 100 多年前备受欺凌的景象<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>华夏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几千年的文明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全都毁在那诸天神佛的手里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>14 亿人口锐减到 4 亿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至低于建国之前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>屋内<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>到处都是尸体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>今天的华夏国<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>已经名存实亡了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>躲在防空洞里的领导人算什么领导人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>木阳悲哀地想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>身为共和国最后的总理<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他满脸疲惫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>腰也不再硬朗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但他还是想走完这最后一程<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>站着走完<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>恶魔在通州与卫戍军交战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>炮火的声音即便在市中心也能听得一清二楚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>战士们前赴后继<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用手中脆弱的 95 式步枪打出和石头没什么分别的子弹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>恶魔穿行而过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>士兵的胸膛被剖开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心脏被掏出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留下一具具零碎的尸首散落在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>金色的雏菊花瓣零落飞散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似乎是在宣告着生命曾鲜活地存在<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>导弹一枚接着一枚发射<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>到了这个时候已经没有人瞄准了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>所有人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论是技术兵种还是文工团都在最前线战斗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>恶魔军团如巨大的齿轮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把年轻的士兵们拉了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后碾成肉酱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>士兵们已经习惯带上一颗手雷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>关键时刻拉响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有的起了效果<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>与敌人同归于尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有的则只是免除自己更痛苦的死亡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>没有人逃避<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有人抱怨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有人聒噪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是沉默的惨烈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>木阳的秘书又一次催促他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他庄重地抹上发蜡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>系好领带<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把皮鞋擦得锃亮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你走吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我决定了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我要和北平在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秘书说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总理<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您是人民的希望<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>所以我才要留下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>木阳的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掷地有声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秘书哑口无言<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他对着这个倔强的老人深深鞠了一躬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>直升机的螺旋桨越转越快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掀起的风吹在木阳的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使他的黑色西服噼啪作响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>都走了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>木阳打开了摄像机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>卫星把他的影像<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>他的声音传递给了每个仍活着的华夏人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>所有共和国的公民们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>今天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将是我最后一次与你们对话<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>恶魔已经突破了通州防线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>对不起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们尽力了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>所有的军人都顶在了一线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他们用血肉之躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抵挡着敌人的利爪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>可我们只是普通人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>撒旦那样存在于神话中的魔鬼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不是仅凭一颗红心就能够抵挡得住<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>中央讨论决定<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向北平投放原子弹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是最好的打击敌人的方法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我们只有牺牲了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>才有胜利的希望<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>国民们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>同志们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>看看我身后的宫殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看看这座城市里所有的建筑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>这是我们华夏民族最宝贵的财富<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>它们挺过了鸦片战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们挺过了抗日战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们历经千年屹立不倒<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>共和国总理木阳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将与北平共存亡<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>不愿做奴隶的人们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>让我们的血肉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>筑成我们新的长城<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>中华民族到了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最危险的时候时刻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>每个人被迫着发出最后的吼声<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>银白色的圆柱闪烁着光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是华夏最大当量的原子弹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它旋转着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>突进着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在空中划出最优美的曲线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我们万众一心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冒着敌人的炮火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>前进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>前进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>前进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>进!!<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2021 年 10 月 1 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>北平沦陷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>撒旦死于人类手中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>10</p>
