 <p>观海用力揉着自己的太阳穴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>许久才开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你确定我们的核武器基地全都失联了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总统先生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>不仅如此<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们还失去了激光武器卫星<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>现在的人类在那些恶魔面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不比一只绵羊更安全<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是谁泄露的坐标<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没有人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>Shit<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>一群废物<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观海愤怒地把桌子上的东西扫了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那些恶魔怎么会知道我们的基地在哪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>你们技术组都是吃屎的吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>没有人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>难不成还能是我亲自给路西法那个愚蠢的鸟人打电话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>告诉他我们核弹的坐标<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>对不起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总统先生<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>特工嗫嚅道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我不知道<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>滚出去<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观海站起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指指向门口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>特工落荒而逃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>观海深吸了几口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重新坐回椅子上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他要崩溃了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如山的重负压在他的肩上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎要把他压垮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>人类已经到了最危险的时候<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>各路神仙的战争如火如荼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每天都有几十份战报被交到观海手中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但无论哪位神祇最终获胜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类都将是最大的输家<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没有任何一匹恶狼会放弃送到嘴边的羊肉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>在此之前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类拥有能与神同归于尽的底牌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>然而现在<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>高高在上的它们终于意识到脚边蝼蚁的危害——人类连谈判的资格也没有了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>观海沉吟一会儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从办公室走了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>基地里的人都神色匆匆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>基地门口的哨兵发现了观海<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>敬了个礼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>然后听从他的吩咐打开了大门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>外面刚刚下过雪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>科罗拉多大峡谷覆满了白色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>观海的脚踩在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>发出咯吱咯吱的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>人类活动减少后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>空气格外清新<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>落日透过晚霞洒下金辉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在峡谷的岩壁上映出或靛或赤的色彩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>观海看得痴了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他紧紧攥着拳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>指甲划破手心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>滚烫的鲜血滴落在白皑皑的雪中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>融出一个殷红小洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>克洛诺斯很愤怒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他挥舞着巨镰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩碎一幢又一幢高楼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼前的猴子除了勉强能接住他攻击的力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎一无是处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但他太灵巧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灵巧得使人抓狂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>卑贱的劣等神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>克洛诺斯怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空闻声哈哈一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>催动金箍棒变大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杵中了克洛诺斯的脊椎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>然后借力后撤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踏上筋斗云乘风而去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>克洛诺斯觉得自己受到了戏弄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是许多年以来未曾有过的经历<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这让他回忆起曾在塔尔塔罗斯的屈辱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒火充斥了他的脑海<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空压力很大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>身后穷追不舍的巨人不同于以前任何敌人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>其能力之强<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在所有神祇中也称得上是顶级<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>即便是自己引以为傲的力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在克洛诺斯面前都不占丝毫优势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>极其危险<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可能会死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>孙悟空想到<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>克洛诺斯高举镰刀劈向悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轰的一声巨响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>镰刃处赫然出现了一圈圆锥形的云团<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空大惊失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抛出了一把毫毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无数分身在巨镰下断成两节<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他化为一只鹰隼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在这细微的阻拦间避开了镰刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>凛冽的寒风刺入孙悟空的肌肉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他疯狂地冲刺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>速度节节攀升<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>刚才那一刻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他明显地嗅到了死亡的味道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>二人一追一逃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从申沪到渝城<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又从渝城到昆仑山西麓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>激烈的打斗横穿了整个华夏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>天空中不时闪过光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金铁交鸣之声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>千里外都清晰可闻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空擎住如意金箍棒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使其延长百米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>横扫克洛诺斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我要你死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>克洛诺斯一把抓住金箍棒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把孙悟空狠狠掼在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>巨镰旋转如闪电般追袭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空急忙收回金箍棒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>立在身前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>巨镰猛地砍在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那无坚不摧的九转镔铁竟是被撕出一道伤口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空向后飞去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>撞在山石之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一身钢筋铁骨都有了碎裂的迹象<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他落到地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>喷出一口鲜血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仰天狂笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>想俺老孙千年前大闹天宫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那老倌的八卦炉烧出俺的火眼金睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>地府的铡刀不能奈何俺一根毫毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便是那如来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺也不是不敢掀了他的五行山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>没想到如今<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟然败在你的手中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哈哈哈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>克洛诺斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你孙爷爷在此<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>来吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>克洛诺斯拖着镰刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>走到孙悟空面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后一刀下斩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>青葱般的手指捻住刃口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>克洛诺斯的脑门暴出青筋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>镰刀却再也无法寸进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>可恶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>你们都得死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>克洛诺斯气急败坏地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他几乎就要杀死孙悟空了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪想到半路杀出个人首蛇身的女人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>聒噪<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>女子冷冷地开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中山河社稷图陡然升空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2021 年 12 月 14 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>地皇女娲顺手搭救孙悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>克洛诺斯陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>11</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我的主<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您怎么看<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐在御座前躬身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>御座上坐着一个玩世不恭的青年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他抠着自己的指甲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不时从指缝里挑出尘土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他只是那么静静地坐着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>和任何普通人没什么两样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但没有人敢忽视他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>关我什么事<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>呃……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐失语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>可那是女娲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是东方三皇啊……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>关你屁事<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>青年把目光从指尖移开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看向梅丹佐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>梅丹佐的腰躬得更深了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎要碰触地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>以后这种事就不要和我说了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我很忙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有时间去陪你们过家家<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>青年淡淡地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你退下吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>梅丹佐把自己剩下的话都咽进肚子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不甘地咬咬牙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身离开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>目光闪烁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>好似看向虚空之中的什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>路西菲尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的孩子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他缓缓开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>好久不见<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>孙悟空抱着自己的棍子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>欲哭无泪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>无论他使其变大还是变小<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那道伤口始终在那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似一条丑陋的疤痕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>老倌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你就重新给俺造一根呗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>孙悟空觍着脸磨太上老君<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你当这玩意儿随便造啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>不造不造<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没材料<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君偏头不搭理他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一脸鄙夷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你把你那破镯子熔了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不就有了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空嬉皮笑脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手偷偷摸太上老君的袋子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君一巴掌拍掉孙悟空的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你这泼猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不知羞<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>女娲笑吟吟地看着他们斗嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角轻轻上扬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>她闭关多年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>已经许久没接触人气了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>二人的行为冲淡了高处不胜寒的孤独<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使她感觉很好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>其实神也是有私心的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也只是强大些的人罢了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>别人想夺走点她喜欢的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想毁灭她热爱的世界<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那她就不能不管<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>女娲这样想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>你惹我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我就给你一耳光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>死了是你弱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>活该<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>就是这么孩子气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>女娲娘娘!<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>一仙官气喘吁吁地闯进大殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>外面……外面一个自称散人的年轻道士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把一条蛇扔在南天门了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>说让娘娘您亲自去取<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>女娲脸上露出古怪的表情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>疑惑地和太上老君对视一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太上老君拱了拱手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>师侄以为应该去看看<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>女娲点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>算是同意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一摆蛇尾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看似微小一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就飞出数里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>太上老君在她身后跟着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼睛就是一亮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是怎样恐怖的道行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>举手投足的动作竟然连空间都被折叠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>巨蟒痛苦地在南天门前翻滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的双翅被生生撕了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鲜血喷涌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>染红了天庭的土地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他头部最坚硬的血麟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被人硬挖了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>女娲看着眼前的库库尔坎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俯下身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手按在他的头上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>泛起青光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随即脸色一变<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那个道士呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>女娲急切地问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>仙官摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>表示自己不知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空挤上前来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>用金箍棒戳了戳巨蟒的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>惊讶道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>库库尔坎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是羽蛇神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>是谁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>居然能扯了他的羽翼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>挖了他的血麟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又活捉了他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把他扔在这儿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>杀了我……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>库库尔坎有气无力地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>求你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空眯起眼睛环视一圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>见没人阻拦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>手中重逾万斤的金箍棒下落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>砸碎了库库尔坎的头颅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>女娲略微出神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>喃喃自语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>陆压<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>12</p>
 <p>热烈的风扬起一团团细沙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天诧异地望着眼前的六翼堕天使<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那天使英俊的脸上明明白白地写着轻蔑与骄傲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这不对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>湿婆天想到<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这应该是我的表情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你挡路了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>贱民<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>堕天使道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天瞪大了眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>贱民<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>他凭什么说出这种话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就凭他背后那些恶魔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>这种垃圾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>自己干掉的不下 5 万<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>很好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你很好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>湿婆天冷笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你成功激怒我了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>年轻人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>你将为你的傲慢付出代价<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法皱起眉头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他还有要事在身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>现在免不了要费一番力气来处理当下的情况<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天起手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻旋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浑身肌肉都膨胀起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路西法能清晰地感受到里面爆炸性的力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>舞蹈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>舞蹈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>舞蹈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>这是属于毁灭的舞步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天的头发随着他的舞动而狂乱地飘散开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他右手所持的沙漏状小鼓一次又一次地轰击——那是宇宙的心跳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>曼珠沙华在空气中若隐若现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>周围的温度开始升高<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路西法嗅到自己的羽毛传出了烧焦的味道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天左手打出无畏印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沙尘随着舞蹈盘旋而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>形成一条巨龙环绕飞行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>梵风吹到路西法身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蹿出一道道火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一点光斑自路西法手心闪现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而后扩张延伸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耀目的光线四射<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>路西法握住长剑末日审判<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身后六翼一振<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全部舒展开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>金红色的曼珠沙华竟被乳白色的圣光吞噬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>晨星之子路西法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便是反叛了天堂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被打入永劫的无底洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>上帝也不愿自己最完美的造物蒙尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法一步一步走向湿婆天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>梵风冲击在圣光之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅起炫目的流火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他缓缓抬起脚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后踢了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金属的铠靴轰然撞击湿婆天的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>嘭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>嘭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>嘭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>一脚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两脚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>三脚……湿婆天的舞姿越来越晦涩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越来越机械<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>轰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天的灭世之舞被从中截断了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>号称开始后就无法阻挡的舞步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第一次还未到高潮便被结束<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>曼珠沙华纷纷爆炸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却只是溅射出不多的熔岩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天喷出一口鲜血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还未触到路西法的身上便蒸腾成赤色的雾气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法挥舞长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>利刃闪过夺目的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩下了湿婆天一只手臂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>手鼓落到了地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>湿婆天的节奏彻底消失了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊啊啊啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>湿婆天凄厉愤怒地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一条暗金色的眼镜蛇在他的身上盘绕蠕行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的脚下突然出现了一个侏儒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他用尽全力踏了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>裂纹由侏儒的身躯蔓延<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大地开裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>露出了火焰的颜色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路西法飞上了天空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>左手紧握深红色的逆十字架<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天睁开了第三只眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>金色的神火喷射而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>路西法举起手中的十字架阻挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>瞬间就化为了灰烬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>神火洞穿了路西法的翅膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大地的裂缝中窜出火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那火焰如毒蛇一般缠上一只又一只恶魔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后从他们的七窍中钻进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灼烧他们的大脑与内脏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法以剑指天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的光束降落在他的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他目光如炬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一如从天堂跌落地狱时般坚毅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>神火与圣光相向冲击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只须臾间便撞在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>宽身的和尚突然出现中间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>左手迎向神火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手迎向圣光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他微微一抓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神火和圣光便熄灭在他手中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>二位施主留这世间一点余地吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宽身的和尚一拍腰间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金铙和后天袋灵巧地飞入他的双手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>收<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2022 年 7 月 3 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>湿婆天与路西法被弥勒菩萨摩诃萨用法宝收服<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后分置地球两极<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2022 年 7 月 4 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>原定袭击华夏长征军的恶魔军团因被湿婆天杀光未能完成任务<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>华夏第一科技研究所全部研究人员安全抵达莫斯科<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>13</p>
 <p>这是世界上最安全的地方之一<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也是人类最后的希望<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西紧紧握住许季的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>久久说不出话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终长叹一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>许季拍拍施塔西的肩膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>木总理生前说过一段话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我到现在还记得<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人活着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>为的就是能在这世界上留下点什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>有的人是为了给子孙留下余荫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有的人是为了留下传千古的名声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我不知道木总理留下了什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但他应该是无悔于世间的吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>若有所悟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>介绍一下<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我旁边这位是华夏第一科技研究所所长<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>李平恺中将<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西伸出手和李平恺握了握<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺神色激动不已<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不在乎面前的俄国总统和华夏主席<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>焦急问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你说的那个试验体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在哪<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西微微一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吩咐身边的人两句<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身便带着许季一众走进了隧道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>隧道很狭窄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>四周的墙壁都是由特种合金无缝焊接而成<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>几乎每走两三米就会有一道机械门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>到处都是机关<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这样防守严密的实验室<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就算是神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻易也进不来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>几人走到隧道尽头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>施塔西验证虹膜解锁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后推开大门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>迎面是一个充斥着淡蓝色营养液的巨大玻璃圆筒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>戴着氧气面罩的男人漂浮其中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身上连接着无数电子感应器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>研究人员不时调制着什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指快速地敲打着键盘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>令人眼花缭乱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这就是……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这就是我们所发现的近乎完美的试验体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>前华夏国中士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我们叫他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>九号<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你觉得对他来说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想留下些什么呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>施塔西嘴角微微扬起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>总统先生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是我们手里所拥有的全部神血了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嗯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你带去莫斯科吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观海坐在办公桌前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>语气听不出一丝波澜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那您呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总统先生<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>研究员疑惑地问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>观海玩着手中的钢笔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>好半天才开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我听说啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>木阳那个家伙死在北平了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些事没开始之前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>华夏是我们最大的假想敌之一<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没想到几年过去了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我却要把世界上最有价值的东西送到莫斯科<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>观海露出了笑容<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我要是也去莫斯科<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>岂不是显得我很没面子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您是说……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>研究员睁大了眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我不走了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观海斩钉截铁地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>这儿还有我的人民<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>总统先生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您是我们的领袖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您没必要这样的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>研究员急切道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我们还有很多事需要您亲自处理<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有必要的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观海淡淡地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我在总统的位子上坐了 14 年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>是米国史上执政时间最久的总统<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你知道尼采吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>他说人的情况和树相同<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它越想开向高处和明亮处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它的根越要向下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向泥土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向黑暗处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向深<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向恶<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>上帝死了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我也该死了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>战斧导弹一枚枚飞向阿普切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又一枚枚在空中爆破<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>士兵们把亲人的照片放在唇间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深深地亲吻上面的影像<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>脸上雀斑未退的孩子狂吼着扣动了扳机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼泪在他沾满灰尘的脸上冲出两道沟壑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>人类是为什么存留在这个世界上呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观海不禁想到<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>既然都已经有了更强大的神了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>为什么还要让人类这种脆弱的物种拥有自己的智能呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>难道只是为了服务于这些残暴的神祇吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>难道人类所能做的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就只有被屠戮吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>这是我们赖以生存的家啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>谁要是闯进来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就算是拼着玉石俱焚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们也不会让他们好过的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>观海从基地中走出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他望着红色的河水<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那曾经是泥沙的颜色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>朋友<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观海开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿普切歪了歪自己的头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有些迷茫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你不怕我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怕<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>那你为什么敢站在我面前<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>因为今天是 7 月 4 日<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>所以<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我不能怕<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>观海举起手中的枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2022 年 7 月 4 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>米国最后的军事基地沦陷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>米国总统观海<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>死亡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>14</p>
 <p>泰兹凯特力波卡把手中的橡木杯狠狠地敲在桌子上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>殷红的酒液从中迸溅出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他微微起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>丑陋的面孔贴近面前的金发男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>吉尔伽美什<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>你是在轻视我的实力吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您想多了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尊敬的夜神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>吉尔伽美什缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>您也知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论是希腊那群蠢货<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是东方那群道士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都不是好相与的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我相信您的实力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但若是伤敌一千自损八百<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>岂不是有些得不偿失<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>泰兹凯特力波卡眯着眼睛打量着吉尔伽美什<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沉吟一番<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你说的倒也有几分道理<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>吉尔伽美什暗自冷笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这种自大愚蠢的垃圾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也是活该被我当炮灰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乌鲁克的英雄王<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们是盟友了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>泰兹凯特力波卡伸出右手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>吉尔伽美什的脸上绽开了笑容<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸出手与泰兹凯特力波卡相握<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>尊敬的夜神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的第一个建议是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>袭击太阳神乌图<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>尊敬的上神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我祈求一把能承载我力量的兵器<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>镇元子看着跪在地上的魁梧男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>感到一阵无奈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>13 天了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不论日夜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个男人始终跪在五庄观前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只为求一兵器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>每次镇元子走到他的面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就会听到他重复这句话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>镇元子被缠得烦了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就派童子轰他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他跪在那里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双膝好像扎根于泥土之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论童子用多大的力气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都纹丝不动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那男人就如一块磐石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>任凭波涛汹涌打在身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>意志之坚定就连镇元子都有些感动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>只可惜他不是华夏人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>镇元子成这地仙之祖无数年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从来就没听说有把法宝传于异族的先例<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>现在还是战时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一旦出了差错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后果不堪设想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你别跪着了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>行这莽夫泼皮之事<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我也不会破格赠你些什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>镇元子头疼道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人似是没听到镇元子的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又一次重复道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>尊敬的上神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我祈求一把能承载我力量的兵器<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你这无赖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怎么不识好歹<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>镇元子恼怒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>举起玉尘麈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地抽了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>只是一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>男人的后背就被抽得皮开肉绽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>尊敬的上神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我祈求一把能承载我力量的兵器<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>男人嘴角流下鲜血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你叫什么名字<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>镇元子问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人眼中一片茫然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我……不记得了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>罢了罢了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>镇元子把玉尘麈抛起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抬手抹去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他手掌触碰到的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>碧玉融成液体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又重新凝聚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一把翠色的短刀赫然成型<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>镇元子把刀扔在男人面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拂袖入观<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>门砰地关紧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人连磕三个响头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道观门前的青砖都沾上了血渍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他拿起玉刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掂了掂重量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脸上露出笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猩红的刺青在他坚实的肌肉上隐隐浮现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>15</p>
 <p>红发蛇身的男人在大殿里踱步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>焦躁不安<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>淡蓝色的水气不时在他身边盘旋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>伟大的皇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我嗅到了伪神的香气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请允许我去铲除他们<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>共工<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坐下<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>为什么女娲能去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我不能?<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>共工愤愤不平<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>就因为我几万年前犯了那点小错<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>坐下<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这样是不公平的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那些伪神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我能感受到他们体内蓬勃的力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>要是能把他们全部吞噬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我立刻就能更进一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>皇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你不能……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>坐下<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲的声音如雷霆般炸响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的能量由他的唇齿间蔓延<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>瞬间席卷了大殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>共工体内血气一阵翻腾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>喉头就是一甜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随即闭上了嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坐在了座位上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你以为你什么想法我不知道<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲冷冷地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你以为你是什么人物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>记着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人外有人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>人间什么样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还轮不到你去管<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>殿下噤若寒蝉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>共工低头不语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼中闪烁着异样的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>阿瑞斯把手中的战矛送入恶魔的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>炸出一片黏稠的血液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他感到很兴奋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杀戮的快感让他痴迷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>对于他来说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>兵器进入敌人身体的触感就如同吸食毒品<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿瑞斯发出阵阵狂笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲向敌阵中心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那里是军团长所在的位置<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿斯莫德感到浑身汗毛都奓了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把毒枪插在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地顺势摆腰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>闪开了阿瑞斯的战矛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿瑞斯咦了一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼睛如饿狼看见血肉般放光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他又一次扬起战矛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右臂狂舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>霎时就是一片虚影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿斯莫德的牛头被战矛刺穿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他痛苦地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>另外的羊头嘴中喷出熊熊火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿瑞斯一躬身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拔地而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>闪开喷吐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中战矛一甩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便抽爆了阿斯莫德的第二颗头颅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>阿斯莫德惊恐地后退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身振翅而飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>杀了你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>哈哈哈哈哈<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>阿瑞斯狂笑着追逐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中战矛不断挑飞一个个恶魔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转瞬之间便在恶魔军团中杀出一条血路<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿斯莫德避无可避<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蛇尾甩出一道风刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身拼命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿瑞斯脸上露出残忍的笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右脚后撤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中战矛绽放出金色的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>巨剑刺穿了阿斯莫德的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>阿斯莫德艰难地转头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看见了一个浑身铠甲的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人一抖重剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阿斯莫德被当胸斩断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仅剩的头颅上双目圆睁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>残留着不甘的神色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你是什么人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>阿瑞斯警惕地问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中的长矛蓄积力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>泛出隐隐流光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>战争<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>长鞭从身后缠住了阿瑞斯的右手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>阿瑞斯一惊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地挣扎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>战矛上的光芒竟有要熄灭的预兆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>瘟疫<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>炼金手炮绽放出湛蓝色的火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蕴含巨大动能的子弹在空中划出一道优美的弧线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>射入了阿瑞斯的腹腔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>神的躯体竟是被生生轰出了巨大的缺口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液狂飙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>内脏落到地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还在蠕动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>饥荒<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>戴着白骨面具的瘦高男人骑着惨绿色的战马疾驰而来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中拖着一把巨大的镰刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>绝望青驹……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>阿瑞斯喃喃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>镰刀的锋刃挥过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天地都旋转了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是阿瑞斯看到的最后景象<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>马蹄踩碎了阿瑞斯的头颅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它打了个响鼻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鼻孔中喷出淡青色的火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>死亡<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2022 年 9 月 2 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>淫欲魔王阿斯莫德及所带军团全军覆没<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>希腊战神阿瑞斯陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>16</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你这该死的杂种<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>波塞冬踏着巨大的海马<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一头长发被海风吹得四散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他鱼尾下甩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>海面如沸腾般翻滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一时间乌云蔽日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>狂风骤起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>空气的流速高到令人窒息的地步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>倾盆大雨不要命地从空中砸向地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎要把港口渔船的甲板击穿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人握着手中的碧玉短刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼睛紧紧盯着波塞冬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他失去了自己的全部记忆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>忘记了自己的名字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至不知道眼前的是谁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但男人知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>自己一定要亲手宰了他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>因为他该死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是宿敌的战斗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有和解<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有妥协<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>有的只是刀刀见血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>和置对方于死地的无限勇毅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>波塞冬举起了三叉戟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一道道水龙卷将海水吸了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缠绕依附在暗金色的戟尖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>给三叉戟镀了一层薄薄的水膜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>惊雷被三叉戟所吸引<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不时下劈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>电火钻进水膜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是出现了交融闪烁的奇异景象<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>湛蓝色的寒光将波塞冬的面孔照得狰狞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>波塞冬暴喝一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>半个身子的华丽礼服瞬间被炸得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他艰难推动着三叉戟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恐怖的能量扭曲了空间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的声响几乎要使男人失聪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>第一击就用了如此杀招<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>波塞冬显然是把男人当成了平生最大的敌人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>三叉戟旋转着疾飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将空气挤压出阵阵爆响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着不可匹敌的气势直冲男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊——<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>男人痛苦地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身上的刺青仿佛燃烧起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>放出暗红色的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他全身的肌肉膨胀起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>魁梧健美的身材给人以视觉上的完美享受<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人用尽全力将翠玉短刀砍向三叉戟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一蓝一绿撞击在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轰然爆炸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>坚实的土地似海浪般涌起波澜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蔓延了整整数百米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>蘑菇云升空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>海港残破不堪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就连停泊的最大舰船<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也粉身碎骨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>碎木漂浮在海面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>建筑被摧毁殆尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>昏暗的光线下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>呈现出一幅末日画卷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人站在深坑中心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>皮肤布满了裂纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液流淌着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>染红了大地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>付出你的生命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>波塞冬<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>男人拖着短刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>开始奔跑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的脚掌踏在地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留下一个个足印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>男人越跑越快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大地都随着他的步伐震颤起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>斯巴达人永不退缩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>没有求和<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>没有战败<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>胜利的荣光永远笼罩着我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>死亡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是我的起点<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>男人一跃而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>短刀插入海马的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以不可思议的速度攀爬而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>海马痛苦地嘶叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却无法将男人甩下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我无所畏惧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>无欲无求<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>男人狂吼着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踏上了海马的头颅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他俯视着波塞冬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如天神降临<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>短刀挥出一道残影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>波塞冬急忙阻挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拿着三叉戟的手臂一斩而飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>名为奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>现在<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我才是战神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>碧绿的光影刺入波塞冬的心脏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>炸出一片血雾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2023 年 4 月 5 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斯巴达奎托斯走上复仇之路<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>海神波塞冬陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>17</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>伟大的拉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的父亲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您决定了吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>泰夫努特恭谨地立在一旁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>这将是不能回头的道路<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嗯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>拉淡淡地应道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我们已经蛰伏了太久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>许多人已然忘记了日光的辉煌与焦灼的疼痛<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是时候活动一下了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>泰夫努特点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狮瞳缩成一条狭缝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>透出嗜血的凶光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>眼前是金碧辉煌的宫殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阳光照射在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巍峨得不可逼视<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>把阿努比斯找回来吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们该和老朋友好好叙叙旧了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>拉走了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一挥手合上了宫门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一抹红色一闪而过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个东西真的靠谱吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不知道<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>吉尔伽美什不耐烦地回答<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双目紧盯着屏幕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指小心翼翼地按着手柄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>无人机空袭计划<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿努纳齐的神祇虽然等级不高<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但胜在和谐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>吉尔伽美什没有把握直接冲上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即使是加上那群阿兹特克的蠢货也是一样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当吉尔伽美什听说人类这种底层生物竟然能借助外力弑神时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便活了心思<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>无人机轻巧地穿行在云间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如幽灵一般时隐时现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是吉尔伽美什用自己的血液换来的东西之一<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是人类的最高科技<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>上帝之殇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>战役的核武器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就是依靠它投放的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>启<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我感到有些不安<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大概是战争的缘故吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即使我们不参加<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也总会感觉到杀戮的气息<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>地母之神安慰地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>投放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>吉尔伽美什狠狠地按下攻击键<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>金色的锁链活了过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从无人机上盘旋而下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如箭射出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>细碎的星光点点散落在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>锁链舒展开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一端环绕着安的脚踝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>另一端顺势上爬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这是什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>天父之神惊怒道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他甩着自己的左腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尽力要将锁链甩掉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那锁链如同附骨之疽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每一块金属小节竟然都开始钻入天父的皮肤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在他的皮肤上留下可怕的伤口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>天之锁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>作用是<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>对神的规诫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>,被捕获者的神性越高<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>锁链的硬度也会随之提高<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越难挣脱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>吉尔伽美什兴奋地把遥控手柄往地上一摔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>忍住笑意道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>朋友们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>同僚们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>时机到了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进军<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>杀光他们<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>吉尔伽美什拖两柄战刃冲在最前方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>砍翻一个又一个护卫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他用力抛出修尔夏加那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着气旋的战刃竟在殿门轰出了一块缺口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>出来啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>你们这群胆小鬼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>卑劣的杂碎<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>吉尔伽美什咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>没有了天父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你们就连头都不敢露了吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>主宰者波罗诺明纳列驼着背走上前去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>安抚地冲吉尔伽美什笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后将手掌放在了殿门之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>灰黑色从他手心所对的地方蔓延<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>染黑了整个殿门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他握紧拳头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只留一根食指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻一点<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>殿门赫然化为一片灰色粉末<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>主宰者摇了摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踏入了宫殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>还未等开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>颈部突然一凉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只觉得地面离自己越来越远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是瞬间被斩下了首级<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>吉尔伽美什<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我早该猜到是你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些就是你找来的帮手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>太弱了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>恩利尔擎着巨斧缓缓摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你不该来的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你将为你所做的一切付出代价<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>吉尔伽美什一句话不说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼睛死死盯着恩利尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩山剑直接劈了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>恩利尔抬斧格挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却被砸得连连后退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>乌图冷笑上前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掌心冲外喷射<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>吉尔伽美什侧移<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>避开了烈焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>回手就是一剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从腕部切断了他的双手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>基恩的水弹打到吉尔伽美什的后背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>炸起一片水花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吉尔伽美什气血翻滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛吐了一口鲜血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他咬牙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>战刃挥得使人眼花缭乱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>恩利尔被吉尔伽美什的凌厉攻击逼得后撤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再后撤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>直到后背撞在墙壁上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他心中划过不祥的预感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>瞪大了双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>双刃发出破空的厉啸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>卡着他的肩关节<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把他钉在墙上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>恩利尔痛苦地嚎叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>满脸惊恐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>为什么杀恩奇都<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>吉尔伽美什一拳打在恩利尔的肚子上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>恩利尔感到自己的内脏都要碎了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>为什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>拳头狠狠地撞击恩利尔的肋下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吉尔伽美什能清晰地听到骨折的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>告诉我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>告诉我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>烈焰灼烧着吉尔伽美什的后背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在他的体表吞吐火舌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杜穆基撒下一片种子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>植物藤蔓刺穿了吉尔伽美什的膝盖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>告诉我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>一拳又一拳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恩利尔全身不自然地扭曲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>生生被重拳打死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>吉尔伽美什怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声音里透着复仇的快感与无尽孤独<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我要你们全都死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他缓缓说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>刺入骨髓的藤蔓被强拽了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他一步一步走到惊呆了的杜穆基面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手起刀落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冰刺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弓箭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>无数攻击打在吉尔伽美什的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他终于坚持不住了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>巨网缠住了他的动作<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>钢索限制了他的行为<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大限已到<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>逆民<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>跪下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>解开天父之神的天之锁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我给你自由<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哈哈哈哈哈——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>吉尔伽美什放肆地嘲笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我就算是跪给野狗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不会跪给你们这群杂碎<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>打碎他的膝盖<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>安冷冷地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声音有着彻骨的寒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>上刑<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你……个……杂……碎……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>膝盖粉碎的吉尔伽美什靠着肌肉勉强站在那里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>瞳孔渐渐涣散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>阳光从他身后射过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留下拉长的影子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>boom<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>火光吞噬了宫殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>2023 年 6 月 2 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>英雄王吉尔伽美什鏖战苏美尔众神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后引爆埋藏的超大当量核武器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>神宫倾毁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>参与战斗的神祇无一幸免<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>18</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>雅典娜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们真的要这样吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>这么做的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可就再也没有余地了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>宙斯语气沉重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>父神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们已经没有余地了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜面无表情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>哈迪斯死了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>波塞冬也死了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就连克洛诺斯都陨落在对方手中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我们遗存的战斗力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>已经无法继续支撑这场战争了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他甚至开始后悔加入这场战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>太惨烈了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>惨烈到奥林匹斯付出了难以承受的代价<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>惨烈到就算是神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也被断绝了退路<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑色的白杨树被阴冷的风吹得哗哗作响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>珀耳塞福涅坐在鬼藤雕刻的摇椅上弹着竖琴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>低沉婉转的琴声悠悠四溢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是曾奏给刻耳柏洛斯的安魂曲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>而如今<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仅剩一条碗口粗的铁链<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>门前的巨犬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>换成了满面络腮的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>父亲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您来了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>珀耳塞福涅冷冷地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>您还想带走些什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>我的孩子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯尴尬笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我想要进地狱一次<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>开启塔尔塔洛斯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你疯了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>珀耳塞福涅瞪大了眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你知道那意味着什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他们可能将再也无法收押<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>宙斯道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>可我必须这样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我已经失去得太多了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的女儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我不能再失去更多<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您原来还当我是您的女儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我还以为科库特斯之后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您就不再认我了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>珀耳塞福涅讥讽道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>您是伟大的天父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我在您的面前又算什么呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>冥后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>冥王都已经死了啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>我还能挡住您前进的步伐吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>珀耳塞福涅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你当初穿着长袍收割麦子……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>闭嘴<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>珀耳塞福涅厉声道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同凶狠的狮子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你不配<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜无奈地摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想说些什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却又难以开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯将要触碰珀耳塞福涅白皙的脸庞的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被珀耳塞福涅一巴掌拍开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>珀耳塞福涅愤怒地转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>寒声道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>去做你想做的吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伟大的天父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>不要再加深我对您的恨意了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>她从花圃里折下一枝水仙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大步离开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一路百木枯凋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>卡戎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>载我渡河<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>五条汹涌的河流穿过暗灰色的平原<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刺骨的风带来哭泣的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐隐约约<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>震颤着人们的心灵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>地狱三判官恭谨站在审判台前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>早在一小时前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冥河船夫就派一只秃鹫通知了他们宙斯的计划<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这计划疯狂得要命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但确实是扭转战局的有效方法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>宙斯走上审判台<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸出右手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>夺目的雷霆闪现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吸引了所有目光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>地狱所有的神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>塔尔塔洛斯的暴徒们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>我是宙斯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>炸雷般的声音席卷了整个地狱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>阿刻戎从苦痛之河浮出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踩着漩涡跳到了河岸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双目透射出嗜血的红光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>恩浦萨的羊蹄猛地踏地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>燃烧的头发火焰直冲天际<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>青铜左足发出了指甲抓挠的刺耳声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>墨里诺厄从虚空中显现身形<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>透明的身躯闪烁不停<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>锋利的尖爪从她的手指冒出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>墨诺特斯的手微微颤抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鞭子把牛背抽得皮开肉绽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>牛痛苦地哞叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>墨诺特斯一把扯掉了牛的喉咙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角满是狰狞的笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>斯提克斯锤炼兵器的重锤顿住了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手臂僵在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我将赐你们以自由<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>唯一的条件<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杀了胆敢蔑视希腊众神的任何人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>塔尔塔洛斯的门轰然倒塌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拎着巨锤的仇恨泰坦狂笑着走了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>愿意为您效劳<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>19</p>
 <p>弥勒菩萨坐在蒲团之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>串珠飞旋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴里念念有词<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的面前摆了两盏清茶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似是在等着什么客人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>笃笃笃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻的敲门声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>进吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>施主<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>弥勒菩萨温和地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>穿着军装的青年小心翼翼地走进来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恭敬地俯身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>五体投地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>弥勒菩萨睁开了双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>施主不必多礼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请入座<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尝尝老衲沏的普洱<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>军装青年爬了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>盘腿坐在蒲团上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻端起茶杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>啜饮一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>只觉得唇齿之间异香萦绕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一股暖流顺着喉咙直到胃里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而后发散到全身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
