 <p>青年精神一振<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不自禁赞道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>好茶<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>弥勒微笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也端起茶杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻饮一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不知施主是何来意<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>青年正色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斟酌再三<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小心道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我想求菩萨一点血液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>不知菩萨能否遂愿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>弥勒起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把窗子打开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>寒冷的风夹杂着雪花吹到屋子里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>炉子里的火焰被吹得抖动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却仍散发着温暖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>施主<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的血和你的是一样的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都是普通人的血液<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>青年啊了一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脸上露出了失望的表情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你觉得生命存在的意义是什么呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>菩萨缓缓发问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>青年思索了一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想起老师对他说过的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不确定道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>大概是为了能在这世界上留下点什么吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>弥勒菩萨笑着摇了摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从怀里掏出两管血液放在桌面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又把自己的念珠放在旁边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>孩子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是舍弃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>不舍弃的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就无法前进啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>炉子里的火焰仍旧熊熊燃烧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雪花飞入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又融化成水珠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>菩萨好似从未出现过一般<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只留两盏空杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>20</p>
 <p>孙悟空很纠结<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他的纠缠起了作用<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>女娲娘娘终于吩咐太上老君修好了他的如意金箍棒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这本来应该是件感恩戴德的事儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可女娲又顺手把他送回了大雷音寺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>造了杀业的悟空被禁了足<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>以悟空顽劣逍遥的性子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>整天被关在寺中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还不如杀了他来得痛快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大雷音寺的和尚很无趣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是悟空的感想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>偶尔八戒过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他就会拽住他的耳朵留他一阵子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>聊天打屁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>谈谈神仙的八卦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>打个扑克<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再吩咐他照顾好花果山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他听说下界的战争很激烈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越来越多的神祇加入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又有更多的神祇消亡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一批又一批<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>牵扯范围之大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎涵盖了世界上的所有神系<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他想起沙师弟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想起小哪吒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想起杨戬那个平时溜得比谁都快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却为了那条笨狗拼命的蠢货<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他突然有点惆怅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想找点酒喝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空跳到寺顶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>观察了周围的情况<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拔下一根毫毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一只小猴变了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他冲小猴吹口仙气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其变成一只白鹤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又把纸条系在白鹤的腿上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸手放飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>白鹤扑扇着翅膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲上了云霄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>天空中阴云密布<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>闪电不时划破黑暗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>豆大的雨点噼里啪啦往下掉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雷音寺前的草地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>泥土都翻了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空百无聊赖地坐在门前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>数着屋檐滴下的水珠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们映着世界的景象<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>迅速地下落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在地面粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>时间已经过去了三天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>飞往水帘洞的白鹤还没回来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>要不是知道自己那毫毛变的白鹤的实力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空还真就以为它被什么猛禽捉去吃了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>悟空<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>有人拍了拍孙悟空的肩膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空转头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>忙起身行礼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您怎么过来了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>唐玄奘笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>端着禅杖站在孙悟空身边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>为师想悟净了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空失语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>好久才叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他一屁股坐在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>容俺老孙劝您一句<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是不要想太多了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>沙师弟如果活着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大概也不想您为他如此<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那你呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>唐玄奘一点儿不顾及师父的身份<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坐在孙悟空身边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你怎么还想这么多<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嘿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你这和尚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺老孙可不稀罕你开导<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空撇撇嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>放下吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>你一直以来改变得太多了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你已经快不是你了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>唐玄奘道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你头上的紧箍已经摘了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我也不再是当初愚痴的和尚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有人会给你念咒了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我更喜欢当初从五行山下蹦出来拥抱我的泼猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而不是坐在这看雨的佛<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空眼眸明亮地盯着唐玄奘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吐出一口浊气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你帮俺问问佛祖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>什么时候能放俺出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺有点待够了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>唐僧笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>惊雷滚滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>孙悟空隐隐听到有什么声音哀鸣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>白鹤艰难挥着残碎的翅膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>躲过一道又一道闪电<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>发出阵阵唳叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>悟空抬头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>才发现自己放出去的白鹤浑身是伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼看就要栽下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空急忙往前走了两步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>接住白鹤残破的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它悲鸣一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>松开抓着的信<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>化为一根毫毛飘飞无踪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空拆开信<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是八戒的署名<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液代替墨水留下一行字迹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大师兄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我对不起你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>没能保护好花果山<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空的心脏一颤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拳头攥紧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓对唐玄奘道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>二师弟有难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺老孙不得不走一趟了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>师父只消向佛祖通报一声便是<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢也不等唐玄奘回应<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一个跟斗踏上了筋斗云<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>疾驰而去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>门口的罗汉看悟空离开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>起身要追<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却见得眼前倏忽出现一个披着袈裟的男子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他举起禅杖挡在罗汉的面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>阿弥陀佛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是我欠悟空的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>孙悟空踏着筋斗云在天上疯狂地飙行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>当初取经的人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沙僧已经陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>曾和他同生共死的人一个接着一个再也无法见面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一定要救下那个呆子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他把毕生的法力都灌注到脚下的筋斗云中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>速度越来越快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>然而五根巨大如山直通云霄的柱子拦在了悟空面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使他不得不停下脚步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>如来<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>泼猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>回去吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>莫要再破了杀戒<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>天空中传来了震耳欲聋的声响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>让俺过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>师弟有难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺一定要去救他<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你这泼猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>既然已经成佛……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>闭嘴<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空暴怒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手里金箍棒舞动起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛然打在其中一根柱子上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那柱子晃了晃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是有了裂纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>咝——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>如来抽了口冷气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>手掌一翻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>压下了五指山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊——<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空双手举起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>赫然扛住了五指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>滚<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空浑身爆发出惊人的气势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他怒斥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天地都为之震动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>去他的斗战胜佛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>老子叫齐天大圣<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>21</p>
 <p>猪八戒挥舞着钉耙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拍翻周边狰狞逼近的亡灵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是他被困在花果山的第四天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>皮糙肉厚的他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>此刻也已经疲惫不堪了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>无休止的杀戮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>无休止的砍伐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>令他的情绪压抑到极致<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>近乎崩溃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奥林匹斯神不知道什么时候多了一群如狼似虎的打手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他们与以往的不同<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>实力强劲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刚一到花果山便掀起腥风血雨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>马元帅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你走吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这儿的战斗不是你能插手的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>俺老猪应付得来<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>八戒把九齿钉耙架在胸前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>一直以来猴哥在前面喊打喊杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大家都忘了俺天蓬元帅的名号了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>老猴子听罢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>满是皱纹的脸上露出了笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踏前一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>八戒爷爷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您是大王的兄弟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>老朽虽然法力低微<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不足挂齿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但是为您挡上那么一两刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>老朽也受得起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>您可不能把我们从这赶出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>因为……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这是我们的家啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>马元帅振臂高呼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>孩儿们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>让这帮垃圾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>知道我们在大王手下都学到了什么本事<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>群猴狂啸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着视死如归的气势冲了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>斯提克斯怒吼着把一只又一只猴子从自己身上甩下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又一锤砸成一摊肉泥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他想不明白<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>为什么如此孱弱的猴子却能有如此的坚持<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>该死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>你们这群该死的猢狲<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>斯提克斯的巨手捏着一只满嘴鲜血的老猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那猴子一口利齿咬上了斯提克斯的肌肉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>斯提克斯抓住它的两只手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>稍稍用力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便撕成两半<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>恩浦萨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>你还想看到什么时候<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>恩浦萨一拳打中了一只小猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猴脑在他面前爆开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脑浆与鲜血混合成粉白色液体洒了恩浦萨一身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他一脸陶醉地舔了舔沾上脑浆的手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阴狠地笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>仇恨泰坦大人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不要着急嘛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这么美味的食物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我要让它们一点点死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>斯提克斯厌恶地看了一眼恩浦萨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中巨锤漫不经心地挥舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>砸飞更多的猴子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>惨叫接连不断地响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斯提克斯狂笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘲讽着猴子们的不识时务<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它挥锤转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>突然感觉手腕一僵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是被人招架住<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不得寸进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哦<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>斯提克斯饶有兴致地打量着面前人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中巨锤又一次砸了过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒钉耙一迎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>接下了斯提克斯的攻击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冷冷道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你可以去死了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>血色的瀑布冲刷着花果山的磐石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将一具具猴子的尸体带到下游<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终送入东海<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>花果山已经面目全非<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>激烈的战斗甚至毁了半个水帘洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>墨里诺厄将匕首送入八戒的后背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>虚化消失<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>九齿钉耙砸到她刚才浮空的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嘻嘻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蠢货<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>墨里诺厄轻笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声音从四面八方传来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒重新举起钉耙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>护在胸前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他如今只剩下了右臂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>动作有些失衡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你很不错了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>斯提克斯拿着一块巨石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的重锤被钉耙拆得七零八落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>和我们三个缠斗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟然还能杀一个<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒冷哼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不搭话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中钉耙挥开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着道道银光杀了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>斯提克斯冷笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将手中巨石从八戒头顶压了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>八戒抬手承接<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双膝就是一软<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嘻嘻嘻<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>墨里诺厄笑着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两支匕首插入八戒的双腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻一扭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>剜下了八戒的膝盖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊啊啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>八戒痛吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>整个人被巨石压在了下面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>锋利的匕首划破八戒后颈的皮肤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液涌了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>结束了啊……八戒默默地想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻合上双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>炫目的金光带着无可匹敌的凌厉气息砸了过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>墨里诺厄大惊失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>瞬间进入虚化<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>然后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被一棍爆体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒挣扎着睁眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凤翅紫金冠在阳光下绽放着夺目的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没有人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可以再动俺老孙身边任何人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一根毫毛<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>22</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>战争<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐的语气中带着怒意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>是谁给你的权利<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>擅自杀掉阿瑞斯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没有人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>梅丹佐大人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>战争躬身道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你最好摆清楚自己的位置<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐教训道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>主既然决定合作<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便是这种低劣的伪神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不是你可以越界动手的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>梅丹佐大人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>战争道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>以后不会发生类似的情况了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>希望如此<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐颔首<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>接下来是华夏金陵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我会与你们同行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>记住<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>主的忍耐是有限度的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>梅丹佐羽翼一挥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>消失在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>战争久久才直起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>上了战马<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他一夹马腹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绝尘而去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只留下四道烟尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>夏日的夜格外地炎热<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>罗宁开了一罐啤酒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是他在一次搜索时存下来的私货<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>到了现在这个时候<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>啤酒已经是很稀罕的东西了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全金陵城大概也找不到几罐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>蝉鸣声在基地回响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>微风拂过罗宁的脸颊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他喝了几口啤酒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有些昏昏欲睡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>宁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怎么一个人在这儿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>女人温柔地给罗宁披上了衣服<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坐下来依偎在他怀里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>有点儿难过<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗宁看着漫天的星辰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>雅涵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你说人类真的会有明天吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span> 8 年了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我从一个高中生变成现在的士兵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每天都在担惊受怕地过活<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就像条丧家犬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>今天坐在这儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>明天就可能埋骨沙场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>永远不知道下一个死的会不会是自己<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我怕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怕有一天失去你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>林雅涵贴着罗宁的胸口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>听着他的心跳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>紧紧地握住了他的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>可这 8 年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不是一直有我吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>她眯着眼笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>高中时候的你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可是说了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总有一天要变成盖世英雄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身披金甲圣衣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>驾着七彩祥云来娶我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>可我不是孙悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是个普通人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗宁苦涩道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我只是个没有任何能力的蝼蚁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随便哪位神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都能轻轻松松把我踩死在脚下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而我什么都做不了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>罗宁还欲再说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却被林雅涵柔软的双唇堵住了嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>罗宁紧紧抱住林雅涵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浑身的肌肉都舒展开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似是要把她整个人都揉到自己的身体之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我爱你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>林雅涵把嘴凑到罗宁耳边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吐气如兰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我有了你的孩子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗宁轻叫了一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小心翼翼地埋下头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把耳朵贴在林雅涵的肚子上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>惊喜道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他踢我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哪会那么快就能听到<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>林雅涵笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>别闹啦<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>雅涵<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗宁捡起啤酒拉环<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我什么都没有<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但是我仍然有这颗还在跳的心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>嫁给我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>敌袭<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>防空警报骤然响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>整个金陵基地都沸腾了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>身穿银甲的圣殿骑士执着长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>排着军阵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一点点推进过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>罗宁手一抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>啤酒拉环掉在了地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>真是可爱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类的爱情<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>巨大的天使鼓掌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘲讽地笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>罗宁翻身而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手紧紧抓着突击步枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把枪口对准天使<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠把扳机扣到了底<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>弹夹里的子弹疯狂地喷射出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后坐力震得罗宁的双手发麻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那天使面前好似有一层薄膜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>子弹打在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>熔化成灼热的铅液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>罗宁绝望了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>跑啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他一把推开林雅涵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>别碍老子的事<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗宁咆哮着把枪甩到一边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拔出了军刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>迎着天使狂奔过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嘁<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐慢慢抬起了手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正握住罗宁的脖子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指陷入了颈部的肌肉之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>罗宁能听到自己的颈椎嘎嘣作响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他张大了嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却不能吸进肺部哪怕一丝空气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尿液顺着裤腿淌了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>滴在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他能听见自己女人撕心裂肺的哭声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那么悲痛欲绝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>梅丹佐拖着他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>到了刚才二人亲热的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从地上捡起那被罗宁当作求婚戒指的啤酒拉环<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>可笑<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐手中燃起洁白的圣火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>啤酒拉环化为灰烬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他继续前行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手一挥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几条光索缠住了林雅涵的四肢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把她吊在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>可爱的小姑娘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>让我看看你肚子里的孩子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>梅丹佐伸出一根手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>点到林雅涵的小腹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你……他妈……别……碰……她……<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗宁从嗓子眼挤出声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>青筋暴突<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>军刀刺向梅丹佐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>白光闪过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鲜血淋漓飞溅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>罗宁的胳膊被齐肘削断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>可以了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>战争冷冷道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中的重剑从梅丹佐后背刺入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>胸膛贯出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>梅丹佐瞪圆了眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>满脸的难以置信<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他双手抓住剑刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声音嘶哑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你们这群奴仆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怎么敢背叛主?<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>死亡手中的镰刀燃起了鬼火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他直视着梅丹佐扭曲的脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>残酷地笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>奴仆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>不<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们从来就不是什么奴仆<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他挥镰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩下了梅丹佐的头颅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天使金色的血液浸染了镰刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>平添了妖异的色彩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>就算是上帝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也将被我带走<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2023 年 8 月 13 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天启四骑士背叛上帝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>屠杀圣殿骑士团第二分团<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天之书记梅丹佐陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>23</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>陈尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>准备执行第 27 次参数录入<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>长官<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>陈尘应道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的手指在键盘上敲打<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>输入参数<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>代码在屏幕上飞速滚动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他伸手挑开了几个开关<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>机器风扇的轰鸣声逐渐增大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>圆柱形玻璃筒散发着荧荧绿光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>赤裸健美的身躯漂浮在营养液中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>胸膛起伏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>若冰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把叶甫盖尼博士叫来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>第 27 次注入可以开始了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺扶了扶眼镜道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>这是我们最后的两管神血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>希望一切顺利<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>萨沙一丝不苟地擦着机炮炮管<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是上面配给他的新家伙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他哼着小曲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>觉得自己就像是古代一夫当关万夫莫开的将军<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没有什么能逃脱我的弹幕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>萨沙得意地想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小曲哼得更加婉转动听<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是手里的钢铁巨兽给他的底气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>让他不需要惧怕任何敌人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>萨沙从衣服兜里摸出一根揉得皱皱巴巴的香烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>打火机咔嗒作响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将香烟点燃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他美美地吸了一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吞云吐雾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一道耀目的红光穿梭而过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>陨石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>在低空飞行疾驰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浓烟滚滚拖了数千米之远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>火焰点燃空气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掀起狂暴的气流<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>轰——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>距离基地几千米外的土地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>陨石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>坠落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>冲击波席卷了人造林<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>树木被拦腰折断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>树林中央留下了巨大的坑洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大地被撞得震颤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>萨沙只觉得脚下不稳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>差点摔下塔楼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他手忙脚乱地拿起望远镜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>对着<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>陨石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>坑调焦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九头身的英俊男子踏出了坑洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金发在阳光下闪烁着耀眼的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他望向萨沙的塔楼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>目光透过望远镜正对萨沙的双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他眨了眨眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灿烂地一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>萨沙端起巨大的机炮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后猛地按下警报<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这个有着撕毁坦克威力的大家伙此刻却无法给他一丝一毫的安全感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一段时间以来安逸的生活让他几乎忘记了曾经的恐怖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而现在<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那支配他全部梦魇的恶魔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重新归来了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>萨沙怒吼着扣下扳机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>机炮口绽放出朵朵焰火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么办<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>老师<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>陈尘焦急地问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>基地里到处是警报的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>红色的警灯晃得人眼花缭乱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>继续<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺沉默了一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坚定地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不继续的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们可能再没有继续的机会了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>王若冰推动操作杆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>针头进入九号的后颈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她按下按钮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神血逐渐注射进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>准备注射第二管<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺叫道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>叶甫盖尼博士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>试验体生命体征如何<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>一切正常<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>叶甫盖尼冷静道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>开始注射吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>钢筒中的神血被挤压注射<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全进入了九号的身体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>体温计上的示数不断飙升<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后竟变为跳跃的乱码<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>四人目不转睛地盯着玻璃筒中的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的皮肤隐隐射出红色的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>周围的营养液都开始沸腾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>门被撞开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>端着枪的哨兵敬了个军礼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>报告<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>叶甫盖尼博士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>李中将<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>莫斯科红场基地传来消息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>施塔西总统要求你们立刻去指挥中心与他通话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请跟我来<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶甫盖尼和李平恺对视一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身吩咐了几句<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>跟着哨兵走了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>实验室里只剩陈尘和王若冰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圆筒内的动静越来越大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>二人也顾不得别的什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>紧盯着实验数据<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>视线不敢有一丝飘移<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>请实验室内人员全部撤离<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>机械的声音响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陈尘一惊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看向雷达屏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>红色的光点已然突破到隧道的一半了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一瞬间千百个念头划过陈尘的脑海<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他咬牙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不等王若冰有反应<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便冲了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在门外把实验室的门反锁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>王若冰惊呼着抬头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲到门口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却无论如何打不开机械门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她拍门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她叫嚷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她诅咒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声音隔着门传了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>陈尘却只当听不见<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>陈尘深深吸了几口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冷汗浸透了衣服<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么可能跑得了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>那可是神祇<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>陈尘沉重地想到<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>有用的人才被借口调离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>多余的人则被留下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我们已经被抛弃了啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>人生命的意义是什么呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>被众神屠杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被幸运抛弃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被一切不可阻挡的东西碾压消亡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>地球已经不再是家园了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它更像是屠宰场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>终结了无数的生命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把无数人生的希望灼烧成灰烬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>你拼尽一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只想要多延长哪怕一分一秒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在这个地狱里苟活下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但这永远是地狱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你能做的也只有苟活<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>舍弃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无法舍弃的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就没有办法前进啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>陈尘眼神清澈通明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他大步流星地前行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>皮鞋在金属的地面敲出动听的节奏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他甩脱身上的无菌衣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绿色的军装被气流吹得微微颤动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>满头金发的男子来到陈尘面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他微笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灿烂如花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我叫阿波罗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你叫什么名字<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>陈尘按动金属墙壁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一个红色的按钮翻了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他也笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是比阿波罗的笑容更为炫目<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我叫人类<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2023 年 10 月 4 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阿波罗袭击莫斯科第一军事研究所<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>24</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>施塔西总统<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>许主席<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有什么事情可不可以一会儿再说<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我的学生还在研究所<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>许季起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拍了拍李平恺的肩膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沉重道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他们已经没希望了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还有九号<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都完了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么会<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺难以置信地问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>根据你们在路上时我们对研究所状态的监测发现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>研究所的防御系统已经全部启动了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>你大概能知道那意味着什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>施塔西开口道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>可是实验室不会损毁啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你的学生里有哪个拥有远程开启防御系统的密码<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季反问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没有……可是……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>确实是手动开启的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季打断了李平恺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>老李<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>节哀吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺颓丧地坐进沙发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指插进头发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>陈尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>王若冰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是他最得意的弟子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如今却是说不在就不在了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>人类的生命在更高的层次来看<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>完全是随手抹杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就连同归于尽这四个字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都如此的疲软不堪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>老李<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我有问题要问你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你一定要实话实说<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您问<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>金陵基地到底有什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>湿婆天愤怒地剖开北极熊的肚子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掏出内脏塞到自己的嘴里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他恶狠狠地咀嚼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鲜血沾到前襟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他在北极已经待了一年还多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一年前他醒来时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>发现自己被封存在坚硬的冻土之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他认不出方向<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只得盯着一个地方挖下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一挖就是 3 个月<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他越挖越艰难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越挖越耗力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>终于<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>挖出了岩浆……</p>
 <p>湿婆天有点傻眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>耗费如此多的时间刨土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后却得到如此戏剧性的结果<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他简直难以接受<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天愤恨地换了个方向<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他拼命地挖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这次的速度比第一次快了很多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他越挖越艰难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越挖越耗力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>终于<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又挖出了岩浆……</p>
 <p>湿婆天回到了一开始所在的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沿着正相反的路线挖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这次他终于没感觉到逐渐增强的阻力了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他大喜过望<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每天挖得起劲儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>终于有一天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他伸手一推<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼前出现了黑色的空洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大概是夜吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>湿婆天想道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他心情愉悦地迈出脚步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后感觉脚下一空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身体一沉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>侧着翻了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天只觉得天旋地转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他狂怒地咆哮着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终摔入了岩浆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>被耍了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天终于意识到不对劲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他发现自己无论朝哪个方向挖掘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终都会抵达软流层<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>岩浆固然只能给他灼烧的感觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但再向下也只是虚耗生命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他想起了之前战斗的路西法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>暗忖那个鸟人大概也被困在类似的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心中无端好受了一点<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>作弊的狗腿子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>湿婆天啐了一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>要不是耶和华助你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还敢在我面前倨傲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>我的神火……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>神火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>湿婆天眼睛一亮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指打了几个印花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒啸一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第三只眼霍然张开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神火喷涌而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>火焰溅射之处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>生出朵朵曼珠沙华<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>振<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>曼珠沙华的烈焰花蕊开始颤动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>迷幻空灵的靡靡铃音传播开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>湿婆天的耳朵竖起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他听到了空旷的回声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就是这<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天为自己的智慧狂笑着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他刨开冻土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>穿梭在岩石之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>空旷声源越来越近<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他重拳出击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>破土而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>滚烫的热水瞬间淹没了他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他脚下不稳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>微微一滑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被激流席卷着向上冲去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>几十秒后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>湿婆天随着狂猛的喷泉被射向天空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>外面遍地冰雪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阳光明媚地洒在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>泛起七彩的虹芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天扭动腰肢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全身舒展开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以舞者的极致优雅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻盈地踏在浮冰之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那浮冰竟然是连晃都没晃一丝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>被喷泉冲上天空的破碎冰盖砸了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>操……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>废墟里伸出一只手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓地推开钢板与碎石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>阿波罗缓缓地爬了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>满身鲜血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>显得狼狈至极<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>该死的人类……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>阿波罗咬牙切齿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>面前完好的金属门在他眼里如同嘲讽的面容<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿波罗站起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踉跄着走到门前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双手绽放出光彩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠地插到门里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他健美的肌肉瞬间膨胀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地发力把门拽了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>面容清秀的女子无力地靠在计算机边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼神惊恐地看着阿波罗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>神血在哪<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>阿波罗捏住了王若冰的脖子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>告诉我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>卑贱的人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神血在哪<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>王若冰摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼泪流下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>滑过脸颊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后滴落到地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅起一片灰尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一只手搭在了阿波罗的肩膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阿波罗身体一僵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>回头望去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看到一张皱着眉头的脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>喂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不要欺负女孩子啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>25</p>
 <p>冰盖破碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冻土崩融<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>三眼男人起落巨足<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在大地上印下一个个脚印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他健美的肌肉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>他坚实的骨骼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随着每个步伐而愈发的庞大伟岸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天的身边围绕着血色的曼珠沙华<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>绮丽殷红的彼岸花颤巍巍地绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又在一瞬间枯萎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>释放出一丝血气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在他的四臂之间盘旋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他的身躯直通云霄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>瑜伽苦行僧的模样透射出骇人的威势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他遍身土灰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>头戴的新月洒落辉光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>暗金色的眼镜蛇盘着骷髅璎珞吞吐着鲜红的信子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是灭世的暴怒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>宇宙在湿婆天的神眼中明灭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>天空中突然多出两道黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一前一后循着声音追来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孔雀在天空中滑行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>发出阵阵愉悦的鸣叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>四面四手的男人盘腿端坐之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>口中吟诵着<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>吠陀经<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>》</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他驱动着坐骑围绕着擎天支柱般的身躯飞翔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>尊敬的湿婆天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您因何召来我和毗湿奴<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天张开巨大的双唇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>炸雷般的声音随着龙卷滚滚而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我要攻克大雷音寺<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>迦楼罗金色的双翅遮掩着阳光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在地面留下阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>王者衣冠的男人站立在大鹏之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哈哈大笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>如您所愿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>该来了吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>观世音菩萨淡淡地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中玉净瓶旋转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那瓷白宝瓶越转越快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>化为雪白的圆影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>菩萨叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>捏住瓶子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只听得甘露仍哗啦作响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拍得瓶壁嗡嗡颤动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>树欲静而风不止啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>殿前的罗汉们合着眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>梵唱的声音绕梁不散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>让人心境安定<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>殿首的佛祖缓缓睁开双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眸子里蕴满了智慧的色彩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他摊开手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脸上浮起一丝笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>该来的总会来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>超脱三界<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不代表就是完全断绝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>藕断丝连<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有点变数<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不奇怪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>毕竟是曾经生活之处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们既然已经脱不了身了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那就轻轻地推波助澜吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>呆子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你怎么样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>咝——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>八戒抽了一口冷气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不怎么样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺老猪这辈子遇过的事多了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被贬下天庭变为猪身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>跟着师父取经<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>历经九九八十一难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>倒真第一次吃这么大个亏<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒靠着岩石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一脸苦相地看着自己已经不能动的双腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>膝盖的地方血肉模糊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>半月板被剖了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伤口边缘的肉都已漆黑腐烂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>显然是有毒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>天杀的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这小娘皮下手也太狠了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>八戒痛惜地摸着自己的腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指小心翼翼地碰触伤口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神色就如同守财奴看到被盗的金子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那女的都要杀了你了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还在乎狠不狠做甚么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空撇了撇嘴道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你这呆子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>谁让你在这死守<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>这破山破洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>毁了也就毁了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以后总有再来的时候<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>反倒是你……害俺忤逆佛祖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>犯了嗔戒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>着实讨打<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空也不等八戒回答<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸手就去拧他的耳朵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>八戒被揪得痛呼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>急忙求饶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>连叫了好几声猴哥才被松开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他一脸幽怨地说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>好你个弼马温<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俺老猪替你守山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>反倒落个不是<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哼唧一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手里钉耙一搁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>倒生起了闷气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空也不说话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直愣愣地盯着八戒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那视线像把刀子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>剖得人肌骨分离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>剖得人直见到真心红血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒心里有点发毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>颤声道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>喂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猴哥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你这是做甚么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一把将八戒搂抱住<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不说什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只叫道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>兄弟<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒身子一僵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后宽厚的手抚上悟空的背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你这该死的弼马温<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>原来也有这种时候<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>雨一滴一滴下落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越来越少<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后终于停止<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>乌云逐渐散开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阳光洒下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照得人暖洋洋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>八戒觉得长衫肩膀有些湿润<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>天晴了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>26</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你来了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嗯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我来了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雅典娜<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯谨慎地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>面前的女神优雅地坐在那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>盾和矛都放在一边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似是一副人畜无害的模样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却给他极大的压力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>女战神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>千变之龙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>智慧女神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乌云与雷电的主宰者<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些称号无一不展示着雅典娜的赫赫战功<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>她是预言中可能取代宙斯的女神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>飞扬跋扈的阿瑞斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>连给她提鞋都不配<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>面对着这样一位女神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尽管她表现得毫无防备<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但奎托斯要是真的傻乎乎地这样就冲上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他也就不可能活到现在了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你来错了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜轻轻道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你杀不死我的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>回去吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯感到自己受到了侮辱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他攥紧手中的碧绿战刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>放低重心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弓下了腰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不试试<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怎么知道<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>冥顽不灵<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜从汉白玉的座椅上起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>庄重地戴上头盔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手拿起了战矛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>左手则拎起那镶着蛇发女妖美杜莎的羊皮盾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>她只是站在那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浑身上下便勃发出令人窒息的气质<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>美丽与英武在雅典娜身上完美地融合在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯看着她<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>内心中生出莫名的自卑感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这不是那些虚伪的垃圾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是真正的神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>猫头鹰挥舞起翅膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在天空中盘旋几圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终落到雅典娜的肩膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它耀武扬威地啸叫了几声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声音竟能让奎托斯明显地感受到其对自己的漠视与鄙夷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯不语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>握着战刃冲了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他跃起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>碧绿的残影劈了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜手中的矛稍稍偏了个角度<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>叮的一声脆响便格挡开了奎托斯的攻击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>太慢了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你的用力方式不对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大开大合固然威猛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但细致不足<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也就只有波塞冬那个蠢货会不知道闪避了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜面无表情地教训道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她平淡的嗓音如同尖刀一般刺入了奎托斯的自尊心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>可恶……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯一只脚狠狠地插入大地之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以此为轴转了 360 度<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>磅礴的力量透出刃尖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>啪的一声暴响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>战刃挥舞突破了声速<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>白色的云环扩散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又被奎托斯旋转带起的气流击溃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜不慌不忙地抬盾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拦住了奎托斯的必杀一击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>神情悠闲得就像是可以提前预测奎托斯的所有动作<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么可能<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯震惊地后退两步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的虎口被震得撕裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鲜血顺着翠色的刀身下滑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>动作目的性太强<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太容易被识破了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜又一次无情地开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯只觉得自己像是动物园里供雅典娜戏耍的猴子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>或是屈辱的奴隶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在面前这个淡漠女神的鞭挞下无力地哀号<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的所有攻击都无效<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的所有技巧都被识破<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>该死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯绝望地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看来你还没有认清楚形势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个世界已经和以前不同了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜一字一句道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>恐惧的宝藏已经被无意中开启<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以你现在的水准<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还不如尽早死了的好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你这宙斯生下的杂种<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>暴君的狗腿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯咬牙切齿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>就凭你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜笑着摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>宙斯的时代<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>那已经是过去式了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>她踏步向前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大地都随着她的脚步震动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狂烈的风跟随着她的铠甲骤起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>清空了战场上的所有障碍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>她如同爆发的火山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒吼着冲向奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯的眼中闪过恐慌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他只来得及举起手中的战刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>矛尖打飞了战刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向下微倾又一挑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便把彪悍的奎托斯掀飞了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯只觉天旋地转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后眼前便隐隐约约出现了拳头的轮廓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>三分钟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>足足三分钟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奎托斯没能落地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是一边倒的屠杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是成人欺侮孩子式的虐待<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>奎托斯脑子混乱成一片<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至都想不起来反击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他就像破布娃娃一般<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被雅典娜抛飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抛飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再抛飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他的一切尊严<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在这碾压中消失殆尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯趴在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身上只有皮外伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却没有了再爬起来的意志<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜捡起翠色战刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>插在奎托斯右手边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她眼睛中似乎有着看透一切的智慧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>斯巴达人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灾难要来了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>她把手中的战矛齐胸平端<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力一握<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>原本坚硬的战矛便熔成了暗金色的液态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>随着雅典娜的动作<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一把与奎托斯原有战刃相同形状的金色武器逐渐成形<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜将金色战刃插在奎托斯左手边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身离去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>27</p>
 <p>毗湿奴将手中的法螺抛起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那法螺冲天而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>体积越来越大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直至隐天蔽日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它旋转着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如一根巨棍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>搅动天上的云<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带起如台风般的漩涡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>佛教诸徒<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>毗湿奴雄浑的声音震颤着大雷音寺的寺门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你们的末日到了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>闪电从云团中激射出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些雷电与自然形成的不同<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是每一道都闪烁着金色的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>闪电劈在大雷音寺的屋檐塔尖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>给寺庙染上了一层金色的辉光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>巨大化的林伽相湿婆天走向寺前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他抬脚又回落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>引发大地的狂震崩裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他吞吐气息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>生出滚滚惊雷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他视线所及<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>百草枯销<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他开口质询<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便是万物倾毁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>时光隐灭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>这才是真正的毁灭之神湿婆天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天第三眼睁开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带有无尽杀戮力量的神火喷涌而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直射雷音寺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是一瞬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就要破开大门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>门开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>头戴兽盔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>腰扎革带的菩萨稳步而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他单手将金刚杵顿在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弹起一片碎石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神火触在上面便消逝无踪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>菩萨双目炯炯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扬声道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>父亲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>退去吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>塞犍陀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你要拦我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>湿婆天的声音充满了愤怒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我名韦驮<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
