 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哈哈哈哈<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>湿婆天怒极反笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>很好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那你就去死吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>韦驮菩萨擎起金刚杵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>相比湿婆天而言<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>渺小至极的身躯陡然爆发出浩大的气势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>梵唱的愿声由他的唇间吐纳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>空灵如斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>愿我亦于半贤劫之中调伏众生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是半劫中诸佛所有声闻弟子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>毁于禁戒堕在诸见<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>韦驮菩萨一跃而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双足踏空而行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他每落下一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脚下便生出一朵莲花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每抬起一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>莲花便破碎零落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转瞬之间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>八十一朵红莲盛开败谢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在天空中撒下一片花影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>于诸佛所无有恭敬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>生于嗔恚恼害之心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>破法坏僧诽谤贤圣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>毁坏正法作恶逆罪<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>迦楼罗展翅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乘着风冲刺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它羽毛倒竖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>锋利的刃爪张开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向着韦驮菩萨的后背抓去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一道人影自大雷音寺的塔尖窜起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那人赤面长髯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一身英武正气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一脚便踏上迦楼罗的后背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中青龙偃月刀舞了个刀花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠地斩了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>迦楼罗哀鸣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的羽毛顺风飞扬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的翅膀从根部撕裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伤口横贯了整个后背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>坚硬如铁的骨头被平滑地切开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>肌肉摧了个粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向下栽去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伽蓝菩萨从迦楼罗的身躯上弹开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>头也不回又冲向第二个阻拦的对手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一刀又一刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>划破虚空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留下残影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>所有阻挡韦驮菩萨前进的障碍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>通通毁灭在伽蓝的刀下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>韦驮菩萨宽阔的脚掌踏上了湿婆天的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后向上方急驰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天如同人类轰赶着身上的苍蝇般不耐烦地拍打着自己的身体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>韦驮菩萨左闪右避<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不时飞跃几番<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>红莲在湿婆天的身躯上绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>世尊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我成阿耨多罗三藐三菩提时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悉当拔出于生死污泥<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>韦驮菩萨生生攀了千米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他看着那愤怒的面孔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角挂起一丝笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他双脚用力一蹬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>整个人如炮弹脱膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>倏然升到了湿婆天齐眉之处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>金刚杵被高高扬起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后拼尽全力地落下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>天地的云雷都被引动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>金刚杵插入了神眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天痛苦地号叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仅剩的一丝神火蔓延上韦驮菩萨的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将他一点点吞噬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>韦驮菩萨双手在胸前合十<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>面色平淡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>浩然的正气油然而生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>吾愿以己身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>护一方净土<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后再无影踪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>金光从神火的余晖中播撒娑婆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>佛语瀚瀚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>痛彻天地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掩盖了一切杂音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>佛说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>形虽殒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然意成<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>28</p>
 <p>湿婆天捂着自己被戳瞎的神眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>鲜血顺着指缝喷涌而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似溪流潺潺不断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是自从他生于这世界以来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>承受过的最大痛苦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>神眼被毁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>对于湿婆天来说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这已经不是简单的肢体缺失了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是伤及根本<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>湿婆天抬起巨足<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠地踢向大雷音寺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狂风将一切阻隔都排空在外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伽蓝菩萨急忙放过眼前的敌人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他拎着偃月刀急奔过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拦在巨足面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那巨足越来越近<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终碾过了伽蓝菩萨的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至没有丝毫停顿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>直到此刻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伽蓝菩萨才真正意识到湿婆天的强大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这位印度教最强势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>最凶恶的古神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这位号称可以灭世的毁灭之祖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这一刹那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>展露了自己最凶恶的锋利獠牙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>唐玄奘坐在禅房里诵经<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>油灯忽明忽暗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>映射着寺外的战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>形势严峻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不容乐观<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是唐玄奘一早就意识到的事实<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>尽管湿婆天曾经被弥勒菩萨收押了近一年的光景<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但那其实是在其最弱的法相时借助法宝的强力才趁其不备<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阴他一把<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>要是因此便小看湿婆天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那将必然是灭顶之灾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>吟诵声越来越急促<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>唐玄奘的心已经乱了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就算继续下去也完全失去了意义<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他结束了吟诵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>合上经文<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>站起身来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雷霆将寺外的天空照得通明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>唐玄奘拿起身边的禅杖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>推门走了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大雷音寺的众佛菩萨大多出关<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>此刻都是面色凝重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>从半个时辰以前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大雷音寺的结界就开始被不断地削弱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>到了现在已然是摇摇欲坠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那些恶道的妖兽魔鬼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也纷纷聚集在寺外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无一不期待着结界的破碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>大雷音寺曾是他们罪恶行径最大的绊脚石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如今则是他们趁火打劫与复仇的最好时机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>湿婆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你的眼被蒙蔽了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>释迦牟尼佛声音雄浑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你不是没有智慧的人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以你所能<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>莫非感受不到这娑婆的悲吟吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>蒙蔽<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>湿婆天语气尖锐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我的眼睛被你的人刺瞎了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你以为这世间真的还和以前一样吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>你的神通何在<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>佛祖的声音高昂起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>短视<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我的神通将会终结你的生命<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>湿婆天愤怒地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重拳轰然击碎结界<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>末法时代<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>要开始了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>唐玄奘端着禅杖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指翻飞打出一个个手印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>千年过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他也算是有了一些自保能力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不再需要几个徒弟时时在身边守护<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他回想起曾经被妖魔掳走<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几个徒弟以身涉险的日子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那时候的他还是肉体凡胎的江流儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如今却是受凡人膜拜的旃檀功德佛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>即便如此<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那几个可爱的徒弟还是习惯把他当成千年前的愚痴唐僧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>时间会磨灭许多东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但绝对不包括真挚的感情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这句话用在唐玄奘师徒四人身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大概是十分契合<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>唐玄奘早就想到了今天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>生活不会一直平淡下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总会有各种各样的情况发生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把一切搅得天翻地覆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这场战争对他来说虽然来得有点突然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但绝不意外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>禅杖击中地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲击波发散出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弹飞冲上来的夜叉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>唐玄奘屈指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的卍字符隐隐闪烁着光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>出<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>随着一声低喝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>唐玄奘指尖一弹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>卍字便飞射镇在了夜叉身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的光芒刚一贴附<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>夜叉的皮肤上赫然青烟四溢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它发出了凄厉的尖叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拼死冲向唐玄奘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>善哉<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>唐玄奘无奈地摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手掌印上了夜叉的额头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>光芒从他的掌心钻进了夜叉的天灵盖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只一击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凶恶的夜叉便抽搐着瘫在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转眼消失殆尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>已经不再是那个只能受人保护的和尚了啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>唐玄奘身后光轮绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>七色的虹彩旋转着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将他的身影衬得伟岸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阴冷的风吹得虹彩泛起了波纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一声嗤笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有人出现在唐玄奘面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你是金蝉子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗波那手中拎着长叉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>面目狰狞地问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>唐玄奘<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那罗刹听了嘲讽地一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼睛盯着唐玄奘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眸子里射出的是看死人的目光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他化为黑影贴身上来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手里长叉直刺唐玄奘的咽喉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>唐玄奘面色凝重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他虽然有了点神通<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但也绝不是什么大能<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>眼前的罗刹王却是湿婆手下成名已久的人物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>更是以杀戮知名<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>要说战斗能力他肯定是拍马不及<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他把禅杖拦在面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>暗影一触即收<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在他身边掠过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>伴他千年的袈裟被撕裂成碎片<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>长叉在他的右臂留下了深可见骨的伤痕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>还是……不行吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你很弱<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>罗波那的脸凑上前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中长叉向下一刺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把唐玄奘的脚掌钉在了地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>唐玄奘痛得抽了一口冷气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他压住心中的惊惧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掌心金光四射<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拍向罗波那的面门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>手指穿透了掌心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将骨头一根根挑折<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>罗波那满脸戏谑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他看着唐玄奘痛苦的表情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角浮起一丝阴狠的笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大圣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>花果山在哪里呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>花果山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>离这十万八千里呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那么远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>不过如果是大圣的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一个跟头就可以到了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那可是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>俺老孙——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那么远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我可能走上一辈子都走不到吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>只要你的梦想够坚定<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>理想够远大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一定会到的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>2024 年 2 月 7 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>湿婆天攻打大雷音寺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>旃檀功德佛唐玄奘战罗刹娑之王罗波那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>29</p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>许主席<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的朋友<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>施塔西紧紧握着面前男人的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>珍重<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>珍重<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季重重地点了点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>战争已经进行了 9 年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从维达开始<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陨落的神祇不计其数<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但总会有层出不穷的新神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>压榨着人类的生存空间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>挪威斯瓦尔巴特群岛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是许季一行人的目的地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们将带着全部研究资料向那进发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那里有人类最后的希望<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>末日粮仓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>基地外下着鹅毛大雪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>几百年未见的暴雪遮掩了前行的视线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这固然是障碍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但同时也是一种保护手段<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>虽然这种程度的风雪可能根本就不会影响神的感知<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但对于幸存的人类来说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>多些心理安慰总是好的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一个即将灭绝的种族还能有什么更多的奢望呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>能够苟活就已经是莫大的幸运了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>全俄的基地一个接着一个失去了联系<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终只剩下了莫斯科红场基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>就算是再愚蠢的人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也能意识到基地已经暴露的事实<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这儿不再是安全的避风港<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而是庞大的钢铁棺材<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>人类最后的大国完了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西站在瞭望台上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看着渐行渐远的军队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深深叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他只是不太甘心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这个出身克格勃的熊一般的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>曾在祖国最艰难的时刻将担子扛起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>到现在已经执政 20 余年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西一手撑起了俄国的强大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如今也将亲手葬送这个国家<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我们并没有做错什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但不知为什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们输了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>施塔西每想起这句话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都有种落泪的冲动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没想到啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是败给你了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>施塔西自嘲地笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>就连为国殉职都比你慢了一步<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他小心翼翼地翻动书页<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看着那跃入眼中的文字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>老泪纵横<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西轻轻开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>假如生活欺骗了你……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>阿刻戎踏着雪走向面前的基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的步伐比山猫更加轻盈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>足尖只是微微地磨平雪花的棱角<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至都没能往下沉那么一丝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是阿刻戎最后的任务<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只需要毁灭这里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他便能重新得到自由<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他在地狱里被关得太久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心中早就已经迫不及待了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿刻戎还没发起攻势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>基地的大门就自动打开了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他微微讶异<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在他的印象里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>其他所有基地都是拼死抵抗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这种敞开大门欢迎的行为<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>简直是前所未闻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>朋友<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进来吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我想见见你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>阿刻戎微微皱眉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他之前听说过有其他神祇死在人类手中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尽管他不认为自己也会受伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但还是有些犹豫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>嗒——嗒——嗒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是皮鞋接触地面的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>男人嘴里叼着雪茄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手里拿着一本书<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大步流星地从基地里走了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我来找你了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西站在阿刻戎面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>爽朗地笑了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>也没比我高多少啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哈哈<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>阿刻戎脸上露出古怪的神色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他感觉眼前的男人与他见过的大多数人类都不一样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>尽管是普通人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却能在神的面前从容不迫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是王者的气质<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我是俄国总统施塔西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类领袖之一<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>施塔西满面春风<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>非常感谢你到现在还没杀我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>但是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我更想以一个普通人的身份与你对话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>记住我今天这句话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是代表全体人类送给你们的礼物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我说——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>操——你——妈<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>施塔西的左臂仅剩下连着筋的骨头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>肉被一片一片削了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>滚烫的热血洒在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>融化了积雪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他的膝盖被敲得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双腿不自然地扭曲着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但他的脸上却毫无痛苦的神色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他靠着仅剩的右臂撑起了自己的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奋力靠在墙边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我会站着死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>施塔西笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿刻戎一脸戏谑地等着他站起身又把他放倒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后上前捏碎了他的右腕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西趴在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼神无比坚毅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他仅靠着腰腹的力量向前拱着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一口咬住了一根电线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>牙齿从根部折断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他满口鲜血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一点一点向上挪蹭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仍然把自己支撑了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我会站着死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿刻戎内心中突然涌上来一股暴戾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他觉得自己在被眼前的人类狠狠地打脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那人类嘴中吐出的每一个字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都如同在他的自尊心上狠狠地捅上一刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他上前一脚踩断了施塔西的脊椎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>施塔西再也不能活动任何肌肉了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>肋骨刺穿了他的心脏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液喷薄而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他只觉得生命即将离开自己残破的躯壳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿刻戎啐了一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一脚踢开了施塔西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他不屑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你还要站着死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>阴影中一只手探了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠地扼住阿刻戎的脖子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>男人盯着阿刻戎涨得通红的脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冷冷开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>他会站着死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>2024 年 2 月 9 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俄国总统施塔西于莫斯科红场基地逝世<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>地狱河神阿刻戎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陨落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>30</p>
 <p>男人缓缓地走在冰原上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他闭眼皱眉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似是在思考着什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>风霜凝结在他的剑上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在上面留下青蓝色的冰花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那冰花映射着点点微光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照亮了男人在极夜中前行的旅途<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑暗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>此刻正处于这个星球上持续最长的黑暗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>帝企鹅抱团贴在一起取暖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>簇拥着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>喧闹着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在这地球上极南处营造出庞大的生态系统<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>能量在它们的皮毛下流动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>散发出的热蒸干了汗液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>白色的雾气在暴风雪中升腾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又化为雪花飞舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>如果这时候有航拍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>发到神战前的 YouTube<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一定会在热门榜上挂上起码一星期<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>数万只帝企鹅不断地旋转着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们中间是有着六翼的男子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这如同军队般的企鹅群在南极的土地上不断推进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>金色的光辉不断从天空洒落下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将它们笼罩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又倏忽散去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>上帝赐我以刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>剖我皮肤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>解我筋骨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刺穿我心脏<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>男人默默地念着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中的长剑一时灰暗一时闪亮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我堕入地狱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>七日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>七宗罪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路西法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抑或路西菲尔<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>男人的眸子亮了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他举起长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一束光穿过暴风雪落在他的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他六翼张开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每根羽毛都在颤动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>发出了沙沙的响声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>原来是你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>九号用铲子拍了拍面前的小土堆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将疏松的土壤拍得坚实<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他举起粗制滥造的白色十字架<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力地插了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>施塔西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span>一个人类<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>墓志铭刻得极其有力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那上面蕴含着磅礴锋利的锐气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>简直要刺伤人的双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>九号吐了一口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我是个人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你也是个人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咱们都是好样的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他深深地鞠了一躬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>厌恶地踢开阿刻戎被拧断了脖子的尸体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>走进了基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号对照着地图沿着长廊小跑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>安全出口的牌子闪着幽幽绿光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐隐约约照亮了基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>左转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>直行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>右转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奔行数分钟后九号终于到达了目的地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他踹开机械门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>走进了中央资料室<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>开机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>调取有关 2021 年到 2023 年金陵基地的一切信息<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>九号掏出施塔西交给他的戒指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>塞进了从超级电脑机箱里弹出的卡槽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>风扇嗡嗡地响起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>屏幕上瞬间列出数百条目录<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>九号一个个点开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从里面寻找着线索<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>很快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他便读完了全部条目<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号微微皱起眉头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无奈地叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些信息太过驳杂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他真正需要的东西被藏得极深<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想以这种方式找到<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无异于大海捞针<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号闭上了眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>揉了揉太阳穴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>调取 2013 年到 2016 年间所有最高等级军事机密<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这次只弹出了寥寥 30 多条<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>九号心中一喜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>点开条目<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>逐字逐句地研究起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一条信息进入了他的眼中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>就是这个<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>奎托斯在神庙前坐了足足月余<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的身边插着一金一翠两把在月下放射出神秘荧光的通透战刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>轨迹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>目的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>境界<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>奎托斯的眸子里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>显现着宇宙的起源生灭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>战刃飘浮了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绕着奎托斯的腰身旋转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>两道流光愈转愈快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后绕成一个巨大的光茧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将奎托斯包裹在其中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>光茧突然下沉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陷入了泥土之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>于你而言<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>生存的意义<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯脑海中充斥着雄浑的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是复仇<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯不确定地答道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>还是拯救<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>我也不知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我需要的只是自由<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有任何人能阻止我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是忘<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雄浑的声音中充满着诱惑性<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>忘<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>光茧瞬间消失<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他把两把战刃倒转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠地插入地底<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角露出了残酷的笑容<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>是杀<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>盖亚<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>告诉我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恐惧的宝藏是什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>大雷音寺中一片焦土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浓烟从各个禅房中滚滚而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空拎着金箍棒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脚步沉重地前行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猪八戒跟在他的身后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>失魂落魄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雨滴打在悟空的脸上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又滴落在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅起一朵朵水花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>击碎一切镜花水月的残梦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空跪在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻端起烧毁一半的毗卢帽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其放在一边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他把手指插入青砖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在上面刨了一个小小的坑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>手指又一次进入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这次坑大了一点<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着浸了血液的泥土出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>进入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>悟空用双手挖掘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>手指上的皮肤在大雷音寺加固过的石砖的摩擦下皮开肉绽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后显出了白骨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>足够埋下一人的坑挖掘完成<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空沉默着把毗卢帽装了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>填满了泥土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>走好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他磕了三个响头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>如来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弥勒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你们还想看到什么时候<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空站起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>淡淡地道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>呵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>泼猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>感知倒是敏锐<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>如来有气无力道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>拿去<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>一本金封经文旋转着飞向悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他两只手指一夹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>接了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我们所知道的全部真相<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都在这里了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>31</p>
 <p>太上老君看着面前的军队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不知道该不该祭出法宝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些实在不像是什么值得他亲自出手的神祇——太没有神仙的气质了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我这是到了动物园吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君有点蒙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>太清太上老君<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>狮头的神祇开口询问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一支箭矢在她的指尖旋转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>呃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君捋了捋胡子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摆出一副世外高人的模样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>小娃娃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你有什么事儿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是你就好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>狮头神祇笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>记住我的名字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我叫泰夫努特<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>她从背后取下长弓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>箭矢轻放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而后瞬间拉满<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的弓弦绷紧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>肉眼可见的能量流散出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扭曲了周边的空气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>红色的微光从一点闪现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地爆炸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陨星般的狂暴冲击向着太上老君极尽迅疾地飙射而去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君眉头一皱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不敢小觑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸手抛出金刚琢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>镯子一颤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>箭矢便收了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但红光却没有丝毫消散的意思<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君低呼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>睁大了双睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脚下步履不断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>疾退向后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那箭矢带有的全部能量失去了载体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凭空勃发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是刹那之间就充盈了方圆千米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>烈焰吞噬了太上老君<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>咳咳咳<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君吐出嘴里的黑烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的胡子被燎掉了一半<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道袍也有破损<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>显得狼狈不堪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你们这群可恶的畜生<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君气急败坏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>袖子一挥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>离地焰光旗插在面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>再来<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>泰夫努特张弓搭箭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>磅礴的能量又一次凝结<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>欺人太甚<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>太上老君暴喝一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>法宝尽出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这座东方仙家的移动宝库<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第一次完全展露了自己的狰狞面目<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>幌仙绳化为一道金光盘缚住还在飞行的箭矢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它如同拥有着自己的生命与意识<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是在空中将箭矢折断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君屈指一弹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将紫金葫芦挑飞在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他冷哼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扬声道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>泰夫努特<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>泰夫努特下意识应答<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阵前一片寂静<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不愧是号称东方最强战力的三清<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>果然厉害<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>拉鼓掌赞道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>可你还有多少法宝呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>凯布利<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>我们的礼物该拿出来了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>凯布利阴毒地笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浑身爆发出亿万孢子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同沙暴的孢子被风吹散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>落到地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>化为一只只巨大的圣甲虫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没经历过这种场景的人永远无法想象那庞大族群的恐怖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如山海般堆砌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>密密麻麻拥挤在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>所带来的是难以抵御的无力感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君只觉得头皮发麻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几未出世的龙首金拐被他端了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太极图也滑入了手心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这已经是不曾有过的危急时刻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他要拼命了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>圣甲虫一拥而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君有些力不从心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太多了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些金甲虫每个个体都不好对付<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而当量变上升为质变时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的能力已经不足以应对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君挥动芭蕉扇掀飞一片甲虫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翻身上了青牛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>还不等他逃脱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甲虫就攀上牛身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>锋利的口器刺穿牛皮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>注入剧毒的黏液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>青牛痛苦地哞叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>四蹄蹬踹的力量越来越小<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>老君<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>我来助你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>清脆的嗓音响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蛇躯的美丽女子优雅游行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中山河社稷图的长卷掷出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐天蔽日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君闻声大喜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒甩拂尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道袍在风中飘舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他足踏牛背腾空而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翻手掷出太极图<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>双图环天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>成了太极的异象<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>冲天的青气与虹光纠缠爆裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摄人心魄的恢宏气场遮掩了天地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>混沌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>随着波纹的不断扩散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣甲虫的躯壳迅速地褪色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转眼就变成了一片灰白<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>无形的风掠过无数僵硬的虫体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其卷成了一捧灰色的粉尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>女娲长吁口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>擦了擦额头的汗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灿烂地展颜一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>终于让我等到你了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>红发男人怨毒地冷笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在女娲身后闪现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弥漫着淡蓝色气息的手掌从女娲的后背刺入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你活得太久了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>美人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>32</p>
 <p>修长的手指搭在了共工的腕上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是三根<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便将其稳稳地卡住<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的手掌再也无法寸进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>共工大惊失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浑身汗毛都奓了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他奋力想抽出自己的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但无论他用多大的力气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都是无济于事<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那手指稳得令人心寒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你想多了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>冷淡的声音在共工耳边响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那手指突然发力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深深地陷入了共工的肌肉中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>骨骼碎裂的声音屡屡不断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那足以开山断金的筋骨竟是隔着肌肤被碾成了齑粉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>共工如筛糠般颤抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>剧痛冲击着他的神经<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他想大声吼叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想要在地上翻滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但他却什么也做不了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那手指不仅是捏住了他的手腕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>更是捏住了他的命脉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>他的灵魂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>皇的权威<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲温柔道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指小心翼翼地抚平女娲后背的伤口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哥哥<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>女娲的脸色有点苍白<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我没事的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嗯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那就好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲轻轻将女娲放下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>站起身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>温润却霸道的气势释放出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>毫无违和地融在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君狡黠地一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>闪到了一边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>凯布利神色凝重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伏在地上发出一声啸叫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无数孢子喷洒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一只只圣甲虫从泥土中钻了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这次的数目更多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甲虫的几丁质壳隐隐闪烁着金属的光泽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>显然是实力有了增幅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>凯布利萎靡地后退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这次召唤是他的极致<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这不单是元气的损耗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎要伤了他的根本<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>超越地球任何一次曾有过的蝗灾的虫群<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>势不可挡地压了上来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲缓缓行走<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把手背在身后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>漫不经心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一切动作都如此的和谐自然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>如果此时有人用尺来量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>则会讶异地发现伏羲的所有步距都是同一数值<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>毫厘不差<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他的足尖落入了虫群范围<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>凯布利努力地催动圣甲虫进攻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的精神力疯狂地流逝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>七窍都开始流血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但那些该死的虫子连腿都没抬一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>虫群失控了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>圣甲虫纷纷退到两边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留下一条空旷的道路<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同古代迎接帝王早朝的臣子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>随着伏羲前行的步伐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣甲虫的动作越来越生涩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直至僵硬不动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它们的身躯迅速地失去水分<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后灼烧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绽放出青蓝色的火焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那一线青蓝色的浪潮紧跟着伏羲蔓延开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它只点燃甲虫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冰冷得没有一丝温度<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君在旁边看着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将那火焰与自己的三昧真火比较<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无奈地摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>苦笑一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>蓝色的火焰熄了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣甲虫连存在的证据都没能留下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么可能<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>凯布利崩溃地吼道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你怎么可能这么轻松就能杀了我的孩子们<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲走到他的面前顿住了脚步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他好奇地打量着眼前各种人身兽首的神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>牵起嘴角<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吐出一个字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>滚<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>凯布利炸得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>埃及众神齐齐退了一步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们已经萌生退意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼前男人的实力好似深邃的海洋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不可见底<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>即便是拉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也没有必胜的信心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阿努比斯和拉对视一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>点了点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咬牙挥动镰刀冲了上来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>黑色的长镰斩出一道真实存在的暗影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凶厉地贴上伏羲的喉咙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲皱眉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摇了摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他左手压下镰刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手随意地抬起一挥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>啪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>一耳光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阿努比斯被抽了个七荤八素<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翻倒在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的鲜血从毛孔中涌出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>染红了他的皮毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>冥顽不灵<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲冷冷道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抬起脚踩断了阿努比斯的颈椎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他的身形突然隐去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>出现在拉的身后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>拉悚然一惊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身躯还未扭转过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就感到一股巨力擎住了他的牛角<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠地下压<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲的膝盖轰然撞击在拉的后脑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的冲击波爆发出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>空间都开始隐隐不再稳定<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>两根牛角折断在伏羲手中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他双手轻翻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其转了个方向<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力刺入拉的后背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>撬开了他的肩胛骨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>拉痛苦地怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双目喷射出金色的日光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>烈焰从他的足底蔓延向上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>释放了灭世的普照辉光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>啊拉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>惊人地上升<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照耀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>令诸天向一旁滚动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>我是众神之王<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>万物之主<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一切神祇自我而来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>因我而成神圣<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>足底越来越近<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终印在拉的脸上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将他踢飞出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你很无聊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>2024 年 4 月 1 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>埃及众神联合共工突袭兜率宫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>除少数神祇外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全军覆没<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>33</p>
 <p>达瓦札的夜从不黑暗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法隐藏了他的翅膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>化为人类的样子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>走在这个曾经属于人类的村落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>曾经贫穷但还算热闹的村子如今静谧无声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>能听到的只有昆虫的低鸣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不知道是不是已经没有人居住了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法推开路边破旧酒吧的大门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他缓步走了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绕开倒在地上的桌椅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坐在吧台之前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>灰尘在空气中飘着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>附在那些烈酒的瓶上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他伸出两根手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拈了个看上去还算干净的高脚杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其擦拭后摆在面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伏特加的酒液涌入杯中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>发出欢快的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>想不到在这么偏僻的地方也能碰到与我相同的旅人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法微笑着开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你身上有我熟悉的味道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我喜欢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>黑发的亚裔年轻人抬起头看着面前的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>牵了牵嘴角<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>算是对他的话作答<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法无所谓地耸耸肩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不觉得受了怠慢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>面前的年轻人虽然只是个普通的人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却让他不自觉地想要亲近<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嘿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>朋友<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你脖子上戴的那个<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>能给我看看吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这个<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>年轻人摘下了颈上的金色的怀表<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扔在吧台上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法拿起怀表<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将它擦亮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>繁复的花纹雕在外壳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>构成法阵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>正中间是一颗红色的晶莹鳞片<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不时闪动着神灵的面庞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他轻轻按动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>打开怀表<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>里面是个女孩儿的照片<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>笑颜轻绽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灿烂如花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>怀表内壁刻着歪歪扭扭的字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似是意在表明女孩儿的身份<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>瑶……这是你的女孩儿<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法饶有兴趣地问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>嗯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大概是吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>年轻人点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼睛里蕴满悲伤的爱意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>可是我不记得她了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法盯着年轻人的眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>捧腹大笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>许久才平静下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他眯着眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>想不到你还是个痴情种子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>年轻人不置可否地摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸手来拿怀表<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>棕黑色的光影滑过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路西法目光一凝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扣住了他的手腕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>想不到你的好东西还真多<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法抚摸着念珠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>语气莫测<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>年轻人挣了两下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没能挣脱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脸色变得阴沉下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他抬起头直视着路西法的脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冷冷道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那又怎样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>脾气还挺倔<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法哂笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他从怀里掏出熔断一半的十字架<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>放在了年轻人的手心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>送给你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你的女孩儿还活着<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他拍拍年轻人的肩膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身离开酒吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>火焰从直径 70 多米的庞大坑洞中向上飞蹿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的光芒传得极远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照亮了夜空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法站在这号称地狱之门的天坑边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>展开了自己的六翼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他纵身一跃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>跳了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>热浪舔舐着路西法的金发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那些火焰对他来说只不过算是情人的爱抚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>天然气而已<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便是燃烧了 50 年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不会有什么区别<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些与他要寻找的东西相比还差得太远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他很快到了坑底<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>视野里充斥着被烧得红赤泛金的岩石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>黑色的圆形低台坐落在坑洞中央<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在高温的侵蚀下岿然不动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就是这里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法面露喜色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>毫不犹豫地踏上了圆台<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>诡异的冰寒隔绝了一切热气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>激得路西法打了个冷战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他举起十字长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣光从天穹直通入坑内<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>笼罩在他的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乳白色的圣光逼得火焰都隐隐将要熄灭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法倒转锋刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力向下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>削铁如泥的长剑刺进了圆台中心的六芒星内<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他撒开长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狂吼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以毕生极致的速度逃离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的羽翼挥舞着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至在空气中摩擦出火光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>身后炎浪轰然喷发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>裂变<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>开始了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>半径数万米的黑色火柱直通出地球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在大气层留下了巨大的空洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大地的震颤几乎传遍整个地球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>大洋沸腾翻滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐天蔽日的海啸吞没了沿海的城市<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲霍然从御座中站起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眸中星辰生灭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他长发飘飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>下躯化成了蛇形<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>祝融<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲扬声道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>随我走一趟玉京山<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>34</p>
 <p>耶和华手一抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杯子滑落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在地上摔得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>路西菲尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的孩子……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华自言自语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想开口再多说些什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终化为一声叹息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他拿起手边那本金属封皮的<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>圣经<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>》</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甩给殿下的白袍男子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>送走他吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>白袍男子恭谨地把<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>圣经<span class=" fw-cl "><span>》</span></span>收好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弯腰鞠了一躬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他轻轻地道了一句阿门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身离开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>雅典娜长矛一抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抽散了眼前的黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她抹了抹嘴角的血迹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不屑地冷笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>潘多拉盒子里难道就放出这么一堆垃圾<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影大概是没有发声器官<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沉默地重新聚集在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但是颜色明显浅了一点<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雅典娜无奈地吁了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又一次冲了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>矛尖爆发出金色的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>穿透黑影的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那黑影一晃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是没过了战矛逼近过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雅典娜不慌不忙地后退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>松手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>战矛下落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>她抬足<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脚尖点在矛尖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>爆发出耀目的闪光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>战矛如风车般旋转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绚烂的辉光将黑影的躯干斩碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雅典娜伸手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>稳稳地握住矛杆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将黑影打成一抹淡雾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这一次聚集明显慢了许多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但最终仍然凝成了实体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雅典娜拖着手里的盾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>内心无比平静<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>她不知道自己还能坚持多久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最强力的战矛被送了出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>现在手中握着的仅仅是一杆次神器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>威力实在是太低——只是一只<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>黑影<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>」</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便逼得她招式尽出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>而在神庙外面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还有无数的黑影撞击着结界<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这些黑影如同嗅到血腥气息的狼群<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凶恶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>有序<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>不惧死亡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们冲击着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>席卷了大陆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>毁灭一切能够毁灭的神殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吞噬着神的信徒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜突然有些茫然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她不知道自己做的这一切有什么意义<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至对自己的存在都有了怀疑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>神是什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>能力强盛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>岁月恒久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可以不用发展任何科技<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仅凭着肉体的强大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就足以毁灭如人类这般发展数万年的族群<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>对于雅典娜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至是全部希腊众神来说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这一切生来就有<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>她从来没有想过有一天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>会被更强的物种堵在属于自己的神庙中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>给以羞辱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>神从来就没摆正自己的位置<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>神之所以是神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是因为有着人类的定义<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>然而弱者赠予的夸赞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>真的能够作为炫耀的资本吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜嘴里苦涩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>决战的信心已然无迹可寻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她拍散了黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这一次它没能再凝聚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而是消散无踪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜回头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看着自己的塑像<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>久久不语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>结界的能量越来越低<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雅典娜不再维护<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>涵收气息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坐在了御座之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>虚空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐隐有清脆的声音传来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>结界破碎了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>黑影涌入了神庙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似癫狂的浪潮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们无声地咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>张扬着突进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>很快便挤满了神庙的大殿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜淡然地看着黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>放下了手中的盾与矛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>她解了铠甲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>卸了头盔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只着一袭素衣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>面对着下面嗜血的刽子手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>来吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>终结我吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的一切力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>一切智慧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都送给你们<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜长发散开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>目光炯炯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影窜了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>鲨鱼一般的黑影掠过雅典娜的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在她的灵魂上噙下丝丝神力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>成千上万的咬噬给雅典娜带来了巨大的痛苦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>她神色如常<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至面露微笑——这是属于神的尊严<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>即便是到了身魂俱灭的前一秒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雅典娜也不想让自己有一丝一毫的慌乱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>金色的流光夹杂着青翠的萤火在大殿中绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>魁梧凶悍的人影手执两把战刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>势不可挡地杀入黑影之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同进入羊群的虎豹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他矫健的身躯隐含着爆发的力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每一刀都将空间斩出波澜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>啪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>耳光抽在雅典娜的脸上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把她打了个趔趄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雅典娜捂着脸颊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>难以置信地望着眼前的男人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>蠢女人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个世界已经和以前不同了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯恶狠狠道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你难道就是这种水平吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>还不如尽早死了的好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜浑身一抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>现在不是宙斯的时代<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>更不是你的时代<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>现在是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的时代<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span> <span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>背靠背<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜下意识地拿起了自己的武器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>后背靠上了奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>亲爱的女神大人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我觉得<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可以给这帮垃圾点颜色了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>35</p>
 <p>路西法的长剑斩碎黑影的头颅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他挥动六翼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在众多黑影中穿梭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这些黑影是被路西法放出来的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的火柱喷涌过后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>地狱之门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>便窜出了这些蝗虫一样的怪物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嗜血嗜杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吞噬一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>尽管他自己也不知道这些是什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但其威力他却是已经摸得一清二楚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>它们简直就是为了屠神而生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>任何神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但凡已经拥有神格<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都会受到它们的袭击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些黑影以神的灵魂为食<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以信仰为食<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们无孔不入<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们无穷无尽——至少路西法还没有见到它们的尽头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法直到此刻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>才堪堪明白为什么那些能决定战局的神祇一直隐藏在背后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这种杀不死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>杀不尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>受神力影响极小的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就算是耶和华对付起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恐怕也不会轻松<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法急停收腹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>闪开了黑影的扑击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>左拳带着乳白色的圣光拍在它的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他一触即退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向后滑行了数十米之远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影在空中穿梭追缉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>路西法则不断迎击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他每次挥舞十字长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都是在真真切切地消耗着力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>转眼之间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的额头便渗出了汗水<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影的战斗技能随着一次次拼杀逐渐增强<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>很快就不只是一味地冲刺撕咬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它们学会了闪避<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至是变速突袭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>可恶<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法手中擎着一面光盾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阻挡着黑影的冲击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翅膀挥动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奋力后撤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他准备逃了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>白袍男子在路西法的余光里出现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他举着一本黑褐色的铁书<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狠狠地向下拍出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>还不等路西法有所反应<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那铁书已然贴上了他的后背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>沉重的钝器砸在路西法的脊椎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他浑身脱力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从空中摔了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>银白色的锁链束缚住他的手脚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把他扯成一个大字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>虚空吊了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>银钉刺进了路西法的手腕脚腕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>进一步限制了他的行为<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>耶稣<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法痛得脸色苍白<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你做什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>白袍的男子淡漠地看了一眼路西法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翻开手中的铁封的<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>圣经<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>》</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>耀目的光从那书中绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耶稣开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>声如洪钟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>撼人心魄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>对天下的人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有义的使他接着有义<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>启示录<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>》</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>在这群黑影环绕的地方用这种方式袭击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这简直是要让路西法死无葬身之地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法疯狂地挣扎起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>银钉撕开他的肌肉脉搏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>划伤他的骨骼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液顺着锁链流淌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>染红了银辉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
