 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>圣洁的叫他继续圣洁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>；</span></span>不义的随他不义<span class=" fw-cl "><span>；</span></span>污秽的由他污秽<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>闭嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>想审判我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就凭你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法暴怒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣焰包裹了他的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血液被灼干<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蒸腾出红色的雾气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他疯狂地扭动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>锁链都开始逐渐松动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>狗一般的坏人进不了羔羊的新——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>砰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>金属重靴凶狠地踹向<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>圣经<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>》</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在上面留下深刻的足印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耶稣的话被堵在了喉咙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地倒飞出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你以为你能审判谁<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>战争冷冷道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甩出长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶稣抬起<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>圣经<span class=" fw-cl "><span>》</span></span>格挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>长剑刺穿<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>圣经<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>》</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>通透了表面坚实的铁皮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>卡在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>差一点便能贯入耶稣的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶稣被这力道打得跌落地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他顺势后退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脚步杂乱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>妖娆的女人甩出瘟疫长鞭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缠住了耶稣的双腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耶稣踉跄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>倒仰在地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>晶莹的匕首从袖里滑入耶稣的手心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刃口泛着莹莹绿光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>显然是抹上了足以弑神的毒药<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他手臂后收<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就要将它抛向战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>炼金穿甲弹破空疾射<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>打在耶稣拿着匕首的手上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轰然爆炸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>饥荒戏谑地吹了声口哨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>硝烟与血肉混合成凝结的雾气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>浸染了耶稣象征着圣洁的白袍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>镰刀抵在了耶稣的喉咙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>死亡盯着那面无表情的脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冷冷地开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你不是耶稣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你是谁<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>白袍男子也不反驳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>露出了嘲讽的笑容<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘶哑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你猜<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>猜你妈<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>十字剑刺穿<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>耶稣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>的头颅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把它绞了个粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路西法愤愤地啐了一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不屑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>早猜出来你是什么鬼东西了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>许主席<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你看这里<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺伸手指着屏幕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>这是赫克尔耶夫博士开采的石料上的花纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>同样的花纹在蓝洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>乐山坑群都有发现<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>许季皱着眉头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>点了点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你的意思是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有什么东西在里面<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺双手撑在桌面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>挺直了身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>许主席<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您知道上帝天使这些神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>与咱们中国的神仙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最大的区别在哪吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>在哪<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>他们不是本土神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>36</p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>本土神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季有些讶异<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺肯定地点了点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我们检索了一切有记录的神话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终发现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论是希腊神话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>埃及神话还是中国的神话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都能溯源出其在地球兴起的过程<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但只有一类神话不能<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那就是犹太/基督/伊斯兰这个体系<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺手指不停<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>点开一条又一条目录<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>图文并茂的论文证实着他的言论<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他点击放大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把这些呈现在许季的面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>语气略带狂热道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他们是凭空出现的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你的意思是……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季抽了一口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>上帝是外星人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺语气莫测<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>许主席知道中世纪时期的教会吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>许季点了点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>表示略懂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大概公元 4 世纪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>宗教裁判所出现在人们的视线中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们暗杀希腊数学家<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刮除希腊科学文献<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在刮掉后的羊皮上书写经文<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺痛心疾首道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他们焚烧图书馆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>当时的教皇甚至公然宣称<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>亚历山大图书馆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每几百年就该烧毁一次<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不仅如此<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他们不但毁坏文籍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>愚民政策也运用得极其纯熟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>火刑台上被活活烧死的科学家<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>数不胜数<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我们知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>之前世界上所有学者研究这段历史<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都限定在政治角度<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可现在不同<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们实实在在地见到了神的存在<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们究竟在掩盖什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺大踏步走到另外的计算机前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>开机调出资料<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的手激动地颤抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>投影出一幅巨大的地图<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>1095 年 11 月 18 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>教皇乌尔班二世在法国克莱蒙召开圣会<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>号召组织军队发动圣战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>夺回本教圣地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杀光异教徒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>14 万人的军队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>于 1096 年 8 月 15 日出发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在君士坦丁堡留了一冬后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>于第二年春天渡海来到土耳其<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他们轻松地攻下了尼西亚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又在多利留姆平原以重骑兵横扫突厥王阿斯兰一世的军队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>7 个月后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣战的军队攻下耶路撒冷的北大门安条克<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>1 年后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也就是 1099 年 7 月 15 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>耶路撒冷彻底沦陷于十字军之手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这是世界上最丧心病狂的屠杀之一<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仅仅是阿克萨清真寺这一个地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就有 7 万穆斯林惨死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>男女老幼无一人生还<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>为了寻找被吞进去的财宝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>十字军剖开他们的肚子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至大规模烧尸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在骨灰中筛取金银<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>70 万人在耶路撒冷殒命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>要知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论是伊斯兰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是基督<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>信仰的都是同一个上帝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这样大规模的杀戮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在确定上帝存在的前提下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎是不可能的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但它的确发生了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>立场问题<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季敏锐地把握到了线索<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>伊斯兰教和基督教<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有一方碰触了有关上帝的禁区<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大概就是这样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>教会的绝对统治在此之后并没有统治更久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>很快便逐渐衰落下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我猜和这件事也有关系<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而这样的事<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在此之后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只发生过一次<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>二人沉默无语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>许季从兜里掏出一根香烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>默默地点燃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他深吸一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吐出来一个烟圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>老人苦涩地笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>就是这次<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>对吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他振奋精神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>走到一个柜子旁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸出手验证了指纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他小心翼翼地拿出一块圆碟状石块<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摆到桌面上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>石块飘浮起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>打出了一道光影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这种黑雾般的生物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就是和上帝一起进入地球的来客<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而这块东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>2015 年 11 月 7 日<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>赫克尔耶夫博士采于土库曼斯坦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>达瓦札<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>紫霄宫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>伏羲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我觉得这种事情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是顺其自然比较好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>青衫白袍的长者端着拂尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>有很多东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>并不是如你想象般轻松<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我希望你能够再好好考虑一下<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您以为那些东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>真的不会杀上这玉京山吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>按照我的方法行事<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是最好的解决办法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它们不是依靠吞噬神格弑神吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>已经消亡的神是没有神格的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我们和希腊北欧不一样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是违背天道的行为<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>此事只有您才可为<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>若有闪失<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我愿散济苍生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以身死担责<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鸿钧深深地看了一眼伏羲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从蒲团上站起了身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那就解除吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>半透明莲花在虚空中绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐隐闪着光泽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灵动的青气在莲花的藕心绕行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翠色莲叶吐了又收<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>万道金光如雨丝般散射下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>其中一道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正打在藕心中央的莲子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>虹彩瞬间充斥了天地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>只是刹那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>莲花变得生动真实起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这是……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>讶异的声音响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>远处雷电交加<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>传来几声犬吠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>37</p>
 <p>孙悟空不耐烦地抡起棍子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抽散眼前凶恶前扑的黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他步履坚定地前行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猪八戒跟在他的身后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>二人慢慢地走<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随走随杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些东西无穷无尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阻塞着道路<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这段旅程甚至比取经更加艰难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但悟空并没有选择腾云驾雾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而是权当旅行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他徒步向前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同苦行的僧人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>因为他心里清楚得很<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的大限到了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总该在最后亲近亲近这个世界<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>最后的决战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>诸神的黄昏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是悟空从金光里得到的信息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>八戒也一样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>光球以难以理解的方式准确地找到了世间全部神祇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>召唤他们参加战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>为了生存与荣誉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>什么狗屁荣誉<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>这是悟空心里的想法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但他还是决定去看看<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他已经没有什么可以失去的了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他一无所有<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>所以他无所畏惧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>冥冥之中有什么东西催促着他的脚步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>眼前的金光依着二人的速度飘着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>指引着方向<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>皑皑白雪上留下两排脚印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>通向极北的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>孙悟空的背影有些孤傲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又有些疲惫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他将金箍棒舞得虎虎生威<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却没有了往日的灵气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>猪八戒在后面看得想哭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他几次想叫住大师兄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却又把话咽回肚子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他能说什么呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>孙悟空的脾气倔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是全天下都公认的事实<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猪八戒不认为自己能劝得住他<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>即便猪八戒知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的猴哥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个石猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个铜头铁臂金刚不坏的齐天大圣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是想要送死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影有时疏有时密<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都挡不住猴子那如意长棍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>两颗金色的流光在奎托斯眼前旋转跳跃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吸引着他的视线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那模样似是在说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>抓住我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这是什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯摸不着头脑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转头问雅典娜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雅典娜摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也是一脸疑惑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯思索了一下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深呼吸几口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小心翼翼地探出手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻按了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>光芒爆闪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奎托斯只觉得眼前一花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨量的信息便钻入他的脑海<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>痛得他怒啸一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>光影在他的脑海中播放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是史诗般的战争场景<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>极具煽动力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你怎么样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜吓了一跳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>关心地询问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯摆摆手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>示意自己没事<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的眸子闪着微光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>热血隐隐沸腾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他指了指另一颗光球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那是别人送给你我的信<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>有点儿意思<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>光球在陆压指尖跳跃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>光线迷幻拉长<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他微微叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拿起了摆在面前的飞刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>为什么要找我呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>世间生灵有这么多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大概也不缺我这一介散仙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>孔兄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你说对吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>说那么多废话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不见你不动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不还是要去<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>孔宣不屑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>也不知道我的五色神光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>对上那些天外来客<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>究竟是谁占上风<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>陆压笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>捏碎了金色的光球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>流光溢散出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没入了斩仙飞刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在葫芦上留下一抹流金<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>罢了罢了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>走一途吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也好见见故人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>莲藕凝聚的人形扭了扭四肢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>生涩的动作逐渐熟练起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哪吒张嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吐出一颗金色光球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>乾坤圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>混天绫等兵器都在身旁摆着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一切都和未陨落之前没有两样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就好像只是做了一场梦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>原来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是为了这个而战斗啊……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒喃喃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼神变得坚毅<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他翻过手腕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看那上面血刺的莲形符咒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角扬起了一丝微笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他伸出一根手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把那符咒抹了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这次<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我有一条命就足够了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>三头八臂破体而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒踏上风火轮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻叱一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踏莲而去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你这蠢狗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬一巴掌拍到哮天犬的头上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>老子还用你救<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哮天犬呜咽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸出舌头舔杨戬的手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>它眼睛眯成一条缝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>尾巴欢快地摇摆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬舞着刀花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>试了试三尖两刃刀的手感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>满意地点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他睁开第三只眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>光芒射到万里的远方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>走吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>老伙计<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>再慢咱们可就赶不上最刺激的那一刻了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哮天犬神气地吠着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抢先跃出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您这是……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>取我的东西<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>男子淡淡道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>细嫩如女子的手指穿透石板<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翻挖着暗红色的泥土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>指尖触及碎石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不一会儿便划开了口子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我帮您吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>大汉蹲下身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>帮他的师父一起挖掘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不一会儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一人大的坑洞便挖了开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>男子的双手满是鲜血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐隐露出了白骨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他伸手去拿坑底的帽冠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却是难以用力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大雷音寺还是这样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>什么法术总会在触及它的时候失效<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>真是不人性<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>宽身的胖和尚笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>帮男子捡起了帽冠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那猴子也是真性情<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那当然<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>男子戴上帽冠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼中满是笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他可是齐天大圣啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>38</p>
 <p>无穷无尽的黑影掠过大地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们没有痛觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有意识<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是不断地杀戮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吞噬神格<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吸收神力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>为真正的降临做着准备<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空大开大阖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把棍子舞得力道十足<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>如意金箍棒虽然不算是什么强力的兵器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但用来对付这些黑影倒是绰绰有余<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空的攻击至今没有过落空——他的每一招式<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都会以黑影的破碎为结局<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是黑影太多了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>多到杀不尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空也知道自己现在的行为无异于送死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他看了如来赠予的佛经<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>里面有着详尽的描述<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些黑影杀倒是好杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至是普通人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都可以给它们重创<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但真正可怕之处在于<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们基数太大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>散后重凝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>想要杀死必须多次毁灭其灵体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而这<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至还不是它们的最强的形态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>死又如何呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>孙悟空默默地想<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>只不过是另一段旅程罢了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>现在这段太苦了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>换一段也不一定是什么坏事啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影攀上悟空的右腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>环绕而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空只感觉一阵阴冷气息透到了骨髓深处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他以足踏地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>震散了黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但腿脚明显不如最初灵活了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>猴哥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咱们退一退吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空不搭话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他跃起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>棍子拉长<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凶狠地抽下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>黑影被打得七零八落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空英姿勃发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>气势如虹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在黑影中来回穿梭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如入无人之境<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他在这片战场大放异彩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但猪八戒却看到了他已经有些颤抖的手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>猴哥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>退吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>呆子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你先回去吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空面无表情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我一个人就足以应付了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>金箍棒舞得只剩残影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>孙悟空左右开弓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>略有些艰难地抵抗着黑影的侵袭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>猪八戒急得头上冒汗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咬牙也不应话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他把九齿钉耙竖在身前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>坚定地站在悟空的身边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>让你走<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你磨蹭些什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>弼马温<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你别想扔下我一个<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>八戒啐了一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>要死就一起死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空不知道说什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他感觉鼻子有些酸涩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>半天张不开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影漫了上来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎要淹没二人的身影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>为什么非要死呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>温润的嗓音响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>八戒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>活着不是更好吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>活着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>才会有希望啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空浑身一震<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金箍棒差点落在了地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这世界上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>并不是只有仇恨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>还有很多美<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有很多有意义的事<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你就是脾气太急<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>行者无疆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你心中的疆土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太狭隘了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>师……父……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影遮盖着视线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但这声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就算是死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>孙悟空也不会认错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空狂吼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>罡气爆破出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金光横扫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>周围的黑影都被清理一空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他清楚地看到那和尚就站在那<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身着袈裟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>头戴冠帽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脸上是慈爱的笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空连忙疯狂地奔了过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重新凝聚的黑影扑上来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又在触及悟空的刹那粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有一个拦得住他奔行的身影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空颤抖着探出手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却不敢再向前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他怕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怕这是梦境<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一触即碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>纤细但有力的手掌握住了悟空的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>传递着真实的温度<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我带来了你的凤翅紫金冠<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>人世间最怕的是什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我说是孤独<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>500 年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>整整 500 年的囚禁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>孙悟空只能望着天空发呆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>没有美酒珍馐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有自由<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他失去一切拥有的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>唯独剩下了一条命<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可能是阴天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可能有刺骨的风<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可能飞沙走石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但孙悟空的记忆里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那天始终是阳光明媚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骑着白马的男子揭开五指山上的封印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路途遥远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还有 81 难<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>齐天大圣变成了斗战胜佛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那天他说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他更喜欢当初从五行山下蹦出来拥抱他的泼猴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而不是坐在那看雨的佛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可大圣失了师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>佛却不会<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>悟空戴上凤翅紫金冠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲着唐玄奘吹口仙气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>定<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>来不及了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>师父<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金箍棒在唐玄奘的身边画了个圆圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>沙师弟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>二师弟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你们一定不能从这圈里出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>保护好师父<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>等着别人来救你们<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>背影无限傲岸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>师父啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就让俺老孙再为您保驾护航一次<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空的足深深扎根在泥土中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把金箍棒指向蝗群般涌来的黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>傲气狂飙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>擅入者<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>39</p>
 <p></p>
 <p>葫芦自陆压手中抛出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把盖一揭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>里面便蹿出一道白光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>陆压微微躬身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>请宝贝转身<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>飞刀祭出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>黑影大面积地溃散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却又在转眼间重新聚拢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>陆压脸色有些凝重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩仙飞刀都不能直接破其灵体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是极少见的情况<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>陆兄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没想到你这宝贝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也有捉襟见肘的时候<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>陆压脸色不好看<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你懂什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孔宣笑笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手一翻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>五根三尺来长的羽毛自手心飘出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>神光飘射而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>穿透黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不知究竟打了多远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>被击中的黑影无一不碎裂开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是不是还算是拿得出手<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>还是不要笑得太早<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>陆压淡淡道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸手指了黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你看<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那些黑影竟是又一次凝集<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们一点一点推进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转眼就到了二人身前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>二人对视一眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都看到了对方眼中的担忧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>孔兄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>此番凶多吉少<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还请保重<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你也是<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>孔宣道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>迎了黑影上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>破<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>老李<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是不是该轮到我了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>主席<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺有些疑惑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>您说什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>我不太懂<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你说这世界上还有多少人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>上亿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>千万<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>百万<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季看着李平恺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>这场灾难就算能过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类还能再次崛起吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>会的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>主席<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺坚定道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>人类是很坚强的生物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我们还有很多科技<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>现在的一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我相信都是暂时的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我们不是地球的主人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但我们不比任何其他物种要差<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论是神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是那些黑影<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>但是不会需要国家了吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>国家<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>主席……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不要叫我主席了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季淡淡道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>哪有什么主席<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>世界上已经没有华夏这个国家了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在这个基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我只是个普通人而已<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不是这样的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>李平恺慌忙道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我们需要领导者<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>许季摆摆手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>爽朗地笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他看着外面逐渐停止的雪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>目光深邃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我累了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>什么领导者<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>要当你当吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我现在只想辉煌地在史书上留下一笔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也好让后世的人提起时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>能竖起大拇指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>谁说老人就不可以有英雄梦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>帮我最后一个忙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>替我装车<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>超重型卡车带着拖挂在雪地里疾驰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>天空已经放晴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阳光照在许季的脸上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>给他丝丝暖意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>居然已经开了这么远了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季笑着自言自语<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>也该看到你们了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>来自外星的朋友们<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>仿佛正为了对应许季的话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>地平线上出现了一道绵长的阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>许季踩下油门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>卡车开得飞快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转眼便迎向了黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>许季下了车<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>翻身到拖车之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他伸手在掌纹感应器上按下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>红色的按钮翻了上来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>上面印着黄色的核武标识<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影似乎感受到了许季的气息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向着拖车涌近<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血腥的气息蔓延扑鼻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>人类是很厉害的物种<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>真的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他们并不比任何神祇低贱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>相比神灵漫长的岁月<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如蚊蝇一般的人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也能够站在这里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>和你们这帮垃圾对峙<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影在拖车边转了几圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>开始上爬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>阴寒充斥了空气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>许季只感觉哈出来的气息都凝成了冰粉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>想要吞噬我的灵魂<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季抬腿踢了踢被幕布包裹的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>知道这是什么吗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>三颗大伊万<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是我们人类送给你们这群垃圾的礼物<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>许季把领带扯掉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>解开了衬衫的扣子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个已经有些年纪的老人此时竟是给人年轻气盛的错觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>老木还得唱首国歌壮胆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>老子什么也不用唱<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>许季一脸痞气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>今天老子就让你看看<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>身为人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不比任何神差<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>来啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>老子就站在这让你们吃<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>许季狠狠地捶在面前的按钮之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>黑影都停滞步伐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>巨大的震动传到基地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>震得李平恺捏着烟的手指都抖了一抖<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>涕泗不自禁地流过脸颊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他猛抽一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把半根烟都吸进肺里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>烟蒂被狠狠地摔在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅起的火星照亮了基地里所有人的面庞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺默默地把手中的自动步枪上了膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后一脚踹在大门的开关上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仿佛这样就能把那大门踹得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大门缓缓开启<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阳光透了进来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>洒遍了每个角落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺大步向前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>自动步枪的枪口指向天空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他扣动扳机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>光辉在他脸上闪烁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>子弹极速上升<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仿佛要连那太阳都打得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他面对着基地中数万肃穆的人群<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>面目狰狞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他用尽一生最大的力气怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>人类<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>人群静谧无声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺吐出声带撕裂的血<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>孤独转过身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>脚步印在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留下奔赴史诗的剪影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>无数上膛的声音重合在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咔嗒声不绝于耳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人们举起了手中的枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>踏步使大地都震动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>人类<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>40</p>
 <p></p>
 <p>通天教主骑在奎牛背上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>穿大红白鹤绛绡衣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手执宝剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>立于阵心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>六魂幡插在面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那幡上面一字未写<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只是迎风飘扬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>初晴的阳光洒在阵上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溢射出肃杀的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太上老君与元始天尊在他两侧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>各执法宝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>加持着大阵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>入目间遍是青气流转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仙云氤氲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这个时候的万仙阵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>才真称得上是<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>万仙来朝<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>」</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>万仙阵前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一半翠蓝旗挥摇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>流光微芒间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>四位道人隐隐入阵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>青衣长衫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>英姿勃勃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>即便面色凝重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却也毫不掩饰他们眉间的精气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>四人抬手祭出法宝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无形的立场笼罩了黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使其动作变得机械<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>红旗挥摇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>赤衣道人踏空入阵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>四人面貌狰狞凶恶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>腾腾的杀气弥漫开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>空气似乎都凝成液体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>黑影在其中潜行的姿态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>越发地晦涩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>有效<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>阵中心的三位道君都面露喜色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>通天教主将手中宝剑抬起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>望东西南北指画前后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻叱一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>钟音长鸣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>传遍了整个战场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>转眼间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>九曜二十八宿便投入阵中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>齐行飘忽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>左右盘旋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们簇拥着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>各色虹光萦绕天际<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>天边霞火万丈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>紫色的电弧在霞云中奔腾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>翠色的刀光闪过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将眼前的黑影劈开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>奎托斯顺势扭转身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把另一把战刃插入身后黑影的胸膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>金光在黑影的胸口爆破<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其炸得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>妈的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太多了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯骂道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你怎么样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜把羊皮盾护在胸口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>挡住了几次攻击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>她退后几步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>站在了奎托斯的身边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怨道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不怎么样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>走<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯捉住雅典娜的手腕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一把把她甩到自己的背上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>足下发力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>狂奔脱离战场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黑影瞬间就淹没二人刚站立的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>接着继续推进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>速度相比奎托斯差了不少<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但无边无际的黑暗所带来的压迫感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俨然超过了任何神威<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜搂着奎托斯的脖子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>感受着他炽热坚实的脊背<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>入鼻的尽是奎托斯的气息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>奎托斯手掌触及的地方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>似乎要烧了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你说我们能活过这次劫难吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜轻轻问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你是智慧女神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这种事应该问你才对吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯脚下不停<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>气喘着应道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜沉默<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后迷茫着叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>什么智慧女神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我已经没有什么智慧了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>如果不是你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我连活下去的欲望都没有<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那时我几乎就要死了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全靠你的耳光打醒我<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你曾经还打得我毫无招架之力<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯闷闷道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我不想继续当神了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>如果一点能力都没有<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是不是就可以安稳地度过一生<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜语音哀愁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>无论是逃亡还是隐居<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>起码我可以与我爱的人在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不用担惊受怕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不用为了这些毫无意义的事情拼命<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>蠢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯淡淡道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>如果没有你我这样的人在前面冲杀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>普通人凭什么安定<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>没有神祇顶在前面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你爱的人根本活不下去<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>活得下去的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我说他能活下去<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜坚定道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>搂着奎托斯的双臂收得更紧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他一定能活下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>因为他是英雄<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯不说话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他看到远方有个山洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>当即脚下变换方向<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向洞穴跑去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>洞穴里有些黑暗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奎托斯好久才恢复视力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他疲惫地靠在洞壁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悠悠地叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜钻到他的怀里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你干什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯有点手足无措<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我的英雄<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜目光炯炯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直视着奎托斯的眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>什么该死的女神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>让他们都见鬼去吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雅典娜坚定道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我要做你的女人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>黑影迅速地推进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎要到了洞穴的门口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>奎托斯望着雅典娜的身后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拳头攥紧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>他拥住雅典娜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>霸道地吻了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>雅典娜只觉得灵魂都融化在这个吻里了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>刀柄击中雅典娜的后脑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将她打晕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>奎托斯轻轻将她放在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后站起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>腰肢挺拔有力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>重拳撞击在石壁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>入口被奎托斯打得崩塌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>彻底封死了洞穴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>对不起<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他转身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两把战刃从腰间抽出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>爆发出耀眼的辉光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>但这是战神的荣耀<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>41</p>
 <p>路西法身上流转着乳白色的圣光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>十字长剑抖出一片片残影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>黑影被打得溃散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>变淡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后消失<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>路西法只觉得自己的身体充满了无穷的力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每一次挥剑都能斩出比以往更加凌厉的攻击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法皱起了眉头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>你觉得怎么样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法叫道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>还好<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>战争声音雄浑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>就是太麻烦了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>虽然现在还看不出来什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可一旦时间长了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总会有破绽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那时候这些黑影可就是大麻烦<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法不搭话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>长剑爆出圣光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>穿透了一条线的黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他展开了六翼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向上飞去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>太阳刚刚从乌云中探出头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>温暖的光洒在身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>填充着消耗的能量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这不对<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法喃喃道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>这不是我的能力<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法的手指划过背后的六翼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拔下一根羽毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他把羽毛放到眼前观察一番<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又捻了捻<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>原本的羽毛为白色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如今却是俨然变为了透明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>圣光从根部向上溢散开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>充斥了琉璃般的羽毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在上面强加了乳白<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>二者外形本就相像<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>激烈战斗时又无暇顾及<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这才能一直骗过路西法的感知<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>羽毛在路西法手中灼烧殆尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>爆发出强劲热烈的白色光焰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>路西法没有防备<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只觉得眼睛被刺痛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>险些从空中坠落下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太强了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法心下暗惊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这充盈着圣光的羽毛就如同一块块在虚空中源源不断获取能量的高能电池<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将路西法的实力强提了一个档次<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>死亡横甩镰刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>斩断了面前的黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>同时左手平举<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向着虚空一抓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>暗绿色的波纹从座下马蹄处向外扩散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>十余米范围内黑影纷纷崩溃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他双腿一夹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绝望青驹嘶鸣一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一步跃出了数十米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>逃出了包围<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>路西法<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>死亡怒道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>这是在战场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你是个战士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不是学者<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法闻言窘迫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>俯身冲刺而下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>绕着死亡飞了一圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>清空了周围的黑影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法高举长剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正准备再次劈落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却意外地发现破碎的黑影没能再次凝结<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>四骑士重新聚在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>均下了马<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>谨慎地握着兵器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么回事<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>瘟疫问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中长鞭抖着旋蓄势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>难道就这么赢了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法摇摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也是一脸疑惑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>绝对不会这么简单<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我感觉很不好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一定有什么我们没意识到的地方<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你们有没有感觉到热……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>闪电划过路西法的脑海<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他睁大了双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>振翅怒吼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>都离开地面<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然而已经晚了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>霎时间<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>地面便铺满了赤红色的光影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>无数流火涌动的手掌突然从地面出现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抓住了饥荒的双足<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>饥荒吓了一跳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随即感受到无比的炽热<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他痛呼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>慌忙掏出手炮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把子弹全都射入地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>炼金子弹接触那一层地毯般光影的瞬间爆发出耀眼的光辉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随即融化殆尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>大地仿佛变成了熔火的沼泽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>饥荒绝望地悲嗥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从足底开始<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>逐渐下陷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>化为青烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>化为铁水<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>饥荒形状的赤色光影自流火中站立起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>举起了手炮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>剑指前方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>迎了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>路西菲尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的孩子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你不需要这样的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>面容忧愁的青年站立在虚空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>语音痛惜道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你终于站出来了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的主<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法戏谑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他浑身装甲破败不堪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的碎发被火焰烫得碳化<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就连末日审判<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都只剩下了剑柄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>看啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的主<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法叫道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你看这大地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看这天空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看这些黑色的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>赤色的阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些都是你想要的吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>孩子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>耶和华淡淡道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你不懂<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>我不懂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>那你告诉我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我应该懂什么<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法怒道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>懂你放纵这些东西吞噬一个又一个星球吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>它们也是我的敌人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>所以你寻找一切拥有生命的星球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>依靠其他生命给你挡刀<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>路西菲尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我的孩子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我无法消灭它们<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只能用这种方法拖延<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>耶和华道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>本土神祇与你我不同<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们只是下等土著<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只有我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>才是唯一的真神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你知不知道你之前身边的耶稣早就被替换了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而那个假货<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>和这些东西同源<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华沉默<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>把我从南极引到达瓦札<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>诱使我破除封印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些不也是你干的吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>路西法冷冷道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>至于人类是怎么发现这些的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我猜你最清楚不过<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法抛了剑柄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直视着耶和华<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眸子里射出逼人的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至使耶和华不自禁偏过了头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>耶路撒冷的圣战<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你其实是站在伊斯兰的那边吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>路西菲尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你是我最伟大的造物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>跟我走<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我会告诉你一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>至于这些<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>耶和华指着脚下的地面道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>让他们自生自灭吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法笑了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>笑得如此灿烂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>主啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你不懂<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我是不是您最伟大的造物其实根本无所谓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>我想要的是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>属于自己的最伟大的灵魂<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>路西法痛吼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指陷入自己的羽翼之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他眼中闪烁着光彩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地将其扯了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这是我的战斗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你无权插手<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>所以<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>请你滚<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>42</p>
 <p>哪吒手心中飞出一朵莲花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻旋着追上雷震子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正垫在他的脚下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雷震子微微诧异<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但出于对哪吒的信任<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>毫不犹豫便踏在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向前翻了个跟斗<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>振翼而起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>受力下沉的莲花接触地面的红光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转瞬间化为一缕青烟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>灰烬都不留一抹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>地面上竟是仿佛铺了一层熔岩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>雷震子看了一阵后怕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心中震撼之余<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>回身感激地对哪吒一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黄金棍上窜出两道惊雷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>劈碎了红色流火中探出的手臂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雷震子抽身后退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>避开迸溅的焰花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>飞到哪吒身边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>更多的红色身影从覆盖一层赤色的大地中站立起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们不再是模糊的黑色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而是有了确切的形体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>哪吒甚至在里面发现不少自己熟悉的人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哪吒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你看那个人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雷震子道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>好像是敖闰<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他飞上前准备细看<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒心中不安<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一蹬风火轮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>紧随其后追了上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>敖闰<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>敖闰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>浑身赤色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>暗金色的光芒在皮肤上流淌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他仿佛是听到了雷震子的呼喊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不自然地动了动身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
