 <p>哪吒甩出混天绫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地将雷震子拉了回来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>惯性甩得雷震子头晕目眩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他刚想张嘴骂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却发现原本悬空的地方赫然爆发出一道火柱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>他们不是朋友<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒低沉道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>而是敌人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不吝将你我杀戮吞噬的敌人<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哪吒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>要不要先避其锋芒<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雷震子叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒内心挣扎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后咬牙坚定道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>再挺一会儿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>等等杨戬的消息<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>杨戬化为一只山猫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小心翼翼地在废墟中穿行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>能掩盖行踪的隐蔽物实在太少<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使得杨戬每进行一个动作都要事先斟酌一番<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>入目间遍是焦土<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>沙石经过了高温的洗礼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>呈现出琉璃化的状态<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>迷幻的光芒闪烁着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>衬得地狱之门更加引人注目<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>山猫如利箭般飞射而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他左扑右跃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>肉掌浅浅地沾地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>好似正进行低空飞行表演的战机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>山猫浑身肌肉紧绷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>腰肢舒得修长<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奋力跃入了地狱之门<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>哮天犬奔行着狂吠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嗥叫声传得极远<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>洒遍了战场的各个角落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>他做到了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒面露喜色道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>他进入地狱之门了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>大地突然震颤起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>铺满地面的岩浆如海浪般翻滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冒出了气泡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>无数红色身影从其中爬了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都是被吞噬过的神祇的模样<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他们越来越多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直到地上的岩浆全部转化殆尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒和雷震子就在他们面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却被无视得干干净净<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>红色凝聚的神祇们向着地狱之门的方向转身急行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>留下一连串焦灼的脚印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬戳到他们的痛处了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒转头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正迎上雷震子的目光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>战死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重生<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脱轨于世界<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再立于沙场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这种即便是顶级的神祇也几乎不可能经历到的事情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哪吒和雷震子却亲身体验了一番<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他们已经不欠这世界什么了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没有神格对这些杀戮者的吸引力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却有着神能力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>从现在开始逃离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>隐蔽起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大概永远也不会被任何敌人发现<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可是哪吒不甘心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>雷震子<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒望着渐远的红色浪潮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>微笑着开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你还记得什么是为将之道吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>定自然之理<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>决胜负之机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神运用之权<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>藏不穷之智<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可我觉得<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是少了一点<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那就是不惜身死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>身死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>我早就不在乎了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雷震子目光如炬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>朝闻道——<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒笑着接<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>夕死足矣<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>哪吒抛出乾坤圈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的圆环在空中盘旋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>微微震颤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>雷震子挥动翅膀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>追着飞了过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他的右手捋过自己的长棍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在上面附上一层闪电<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>黄金棍插入乾坤圈的圆心处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟飘浮起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>二者化为一体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>开始极速转动起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>金白色的球形闪电狂飙突进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道道雷火外窜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>莲<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒大喝一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>莲花从他的掌心绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眨眼间便铺满了战场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>花瓣如卫星般围绕着电球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>切割着赤色的身躯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒嘴角带了血迹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>但目光却越来越清明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他收回三头八臂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吐出火枣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力地将其弹向雷震子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雷震子伸手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>稳稳当当接住火枣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他下落<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不管那赤色阴影能否听懂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>微笑着道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你们太多余了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>火枣按入电球<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金光爆炸开来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雷霆万钧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>43</p>
 <p>山猫的身体逐渐变大<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>褐色的毛发顺着毛孔收缩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他直立起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终化为了一个英俊的男子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>红色的光线照亮杨戬的面庞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>三尖两刃刀从袖中滑到手心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被他紧紧握住<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他收敛气息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将自己的感知控制在三米以内<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是最精准的距离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在这个范围内<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便是蚊蝇也逃不过他手中的锋刃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬放眼在坑洞中搜索<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>视线所及<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>全都是破碎的黑色石块<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些石块看似毫无章法<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却隐隐使人感觉其中必有内在的联系<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这是一种很玄妙的感觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>譬如你看到有兄弟邻座<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便可能长相相差很多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你也会明显地感受到二者之间与其他人毫不类似的关系<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而在这地狱之门中有遍地的<span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>兄弟<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>」</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们就像是有意识的生命一般<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>通过某种方式<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向杨戬传达着其共属同源的信息<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>火光四溢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却碰触不到那石块分毫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凡有接近的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都在几厘米外熄灭<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那些碎石好似顶着护罩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把所有的烈焰都隔绝在外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬走上前去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弯腰抓起了一块碎石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>彻骨的冰寒刺入他的皮肤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>几乎要凝固了血液<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬眼中闪烁着异样的光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把碎石拿到眼前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>观察着上面刻下的文字<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是一种不同于地球上任何语系的奇特花纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仅是寥寥几笔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便透出了厚重凌厉的气势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仿佛其中被枷锁束缚了一头凶兽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>有意思<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬有些兴奋<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把石块上有着文字的一面朝上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小心翼翼地放在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>然后站起身子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>小跑着走到另外的碎石前将其捡起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>石块上是与之前完全不同的花纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>透出来的是一种杨戬无法形容的感觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>温和又拒人于千里之外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他来不及细细琢磨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把石块塞入袖子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又去捡更多的石块<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不到一分钟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杨戬的袖子就装满了石块<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他把石块搬回最初的位置<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>堆成一个不高的小山坡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他坐在坡前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拿起碎石<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一块一块地比对<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>寻找能够契合在一起的锯齿边缘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>金光闪过<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两块碎石黏合在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>表面氤氲着浮动的光华<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬面露喜色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>逐一筛选<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>能契合的石块被放置一堆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不能契合的则留在身后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>很快就累积了一堆较大的石块<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他继续拼接<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终拼成了一块墨色的石板<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>花纹状的文字细致地挤在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>勾勒出部分三角的暗红色线段<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬无法形容那种感觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无数种情绪扑面而来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>温和<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>暴戾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>悲哀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>孤独<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>恐惧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>、</span></span>慈爱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些东西混合在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲刷着杨戬的大脑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬甩甩头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深呼吸几口平复了心情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>退后离开了那块石板<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他转身寻找<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一刻钟不到的时间里就聚集了所有的石块<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这些石块微微震颤着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>相互共鸣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬继续拼接<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>或许是石块愈来愈少<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>速度和之前相比要快了许多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>暗红色的线段延伸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>更多的情绪混合在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>纠结成了一面网络<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>随着情绪种类的增加<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杨戬感受到的压力却少了很多<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬也不知道拼这些东西有什么用处<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他只是凭着冥冥中的第六感机械地做着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>不知过了多久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>黑色的圆台终于成型<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>无尽的寒意从圆台向外散发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将赤金色的岩壁都扑成了原本的灰色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>六芒星闪烁着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每个花纹上都似乎涌动着无尽的力量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>杨戬仿佛能看到无数透明的丝线在触摸着整个坑洞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但他感觉还是缺少了什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬伸出手抚过六芒星中央被刺穿留下的剑痕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心思一动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拿过了放在一边的三尖两刃刀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他浑身肌肉膨胀起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力将兵器插了进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>接着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他体会到了不可匹敌的吸引力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬大惊失色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>急忙抽身后退<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>只见三尖两刃刀缓缓沉入其中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被剑痕吞噬殆尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>彻底消失在杨戬的感知里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>杨戬一阵心疼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这武器陪他数千年<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乃是龙吉公主赠予<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但与此相比<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>杨戬更多感受到的是心悸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心悸于武器消失得诡异<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>它已经很仁慈了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没有将你的灵魂一并吞入其中<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>温文尔雅的声音响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>杨戬浑身紧绷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地转过身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看到黑色头发的男子闲庭信步地向他走来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他眯起眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看清了来人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>才松了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>是你<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>前辈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>很久不见了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>男子微笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸出手指虚点了下黑色的圆台<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>您也是为它而来<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>没错<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬坦诚道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>可我不知道究竟怎么做<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>仅仅是把它拼在一起了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>男子走上前去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蹲在圆台边上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼神迷离<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他用手掌抹去了圆台上的灰尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我知道<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把背包甩到身前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手脚麻利地拉开了拉链<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他伸手进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掏出了五根散发着耀目虹光的羽毛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>置入六芒星中央的剑痕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>圆台发出了嗡嗡低吟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>红光变得热烈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从六芒星的刻痕中外溢出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这羽毛是……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬瞪大了双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>红色葫芦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色扁拐<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>青色宝剑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>各式各样的兵器被男子从包里掏了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又投入剑痕之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>黑色圆台如同巨大的熔炉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>对这些兵器一概来者不拒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>红光已经达到了刺眼的地步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>衬得地狱之门都黯淡下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>如意金箍棒<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬骇然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一把抓住了男子的手腕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你从哪里得到的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>俺给他的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>一只手拍到杨戬的肩上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>压他坐了下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>真君<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看着就好了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>男子褪下了手腕上戴着的佛珠<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又把熔了一半的十字架投入进去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>光线突然收敛起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>变得深沉厚重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>男子最后从包里摸索了一番<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掏出块怀表<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后把包扔到了一边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他从怀表中抽出一张照片<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>温柔地贴身放好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后深吸口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把怀表按入了剑痕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>圆台炸成了一抹光尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>大地开始疯狂地震颤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>杨戬只感觉一阵目眩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他什么也看不清楚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只能看到无穷无尽的光明<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我觉得<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类的科技是这个世界上最美的东西了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>渺远的声音钻入杨戬的耳朵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>就设计成这个样子吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>光芒散尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>巨大的多管重机枪被男子抱在怀里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他扣动扳机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>枪管开始疯狂地旋转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>赤金色的符文在枪身闪烁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吸收着空间中的全部能量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>杨戬仿佛看到了一头正在吞吐气息的洪荒巨兽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>光弹飙射出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在枪口绽放出绚丽夺目的死亡之花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>44</p>
 <p>金色的鳞片开合<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吸吮着空间中的能量<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>光线似乎变为实体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>被虚空中的细流引导着渗入蛇尾之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在上面附了一层七色的光膜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>周围一片寂静<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就连风都骤然停了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲怒啸一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>蛇尾在虚空中荡起一片波纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>以无限狂暴的气势甩向耶和华<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华面色凝重<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>急忙抬手格挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>乳白色的圣光在他身前凝聚成护盾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>蛇尾狠狠地抽在上面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅射出一拨虹彩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>接触的瞬间就将其打得粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>那蛇尾势头不减<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>紧接着便拍在了耶和华的掌心<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把他打飞出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华向后踏了足足七八步才止住后退的势头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他只觉得喉头一甜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>血气在胸膛里翻滚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华强压下暗伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扬声道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>伏羲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你就算是杀了我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不会改变什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>阴影军团是你我共同的敌人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>希望你搞清楚这一点<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这个星球是首要的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>其次才是你我的私人恩怨<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你也有脸提这个星球<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲怒道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而后身形闪烁<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>逼到了耶和华面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重拳砸了下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华接住伏羲的手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>往身侧一推<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>腰肢微微一扭就避开了攻击<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他顺势提拉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>欺身便是膝撞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正迎上又一次扬起的蛇尾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>铺满了圣光的膝盖砸得鳞片迸裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲痛呼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>肌肉一紧一舒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着青气的碎麟就旋转着喷射而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耶和华第二次抬腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只觉得一阵剧痛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>急忙瞬移退开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他低头看一眼伤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟发现连骨骼都布满了裂痕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>要知道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神与人之间的差距不仅仅是拥有仙术或是神力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>更体现在肉体之上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>能把耶和华打得骨裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恐怕就算是卡尔臼炮也难以做到<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华咬牙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心知没有了回旋的余地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也放开了手脚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>白焰攀绕他的四肢跃动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>散发出的气息圣洁无比<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却隐隐蕴含着杀机<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>那你就死吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>耶和华道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>一枚枚光球射出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将阴影拦腰撕裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后点燃它们的灵魂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号看着阴影被溶蚀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>消失在光尘之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>内心中充斥着酸涩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这些都是曾经鲜活的生命啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>即便是已经化为了这种东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>即便已经没有了身为人或者神的意识<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他们的任何一丝荣耀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不应该被埋没在历史的长河中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他们曾经是英雄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>现在也是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但他们必须去死<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这不应该是属于他们的结局<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>太漠然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甚至毫不体面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>连尸骨都将不复存在<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这是战争<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>战争里从来就没有同情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>九号很厌恶一句话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span>历史的车轮滚滚向前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>但事实就是如此<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它滚滚向前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>碾碎一切螳臂当车者<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无论是人还是神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>爆炸声此起彼伏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>红色抑或黑色的阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都在子弹构成的浪潮中被拍得连渣都不剩<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>时间一分一秒地过去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>九号扣动扳机的手指都有些麻了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>阴影还是如扑火的飞蛾一样前赴后继<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>尽管如此<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他却能明显地感受到压力正渐渐变小<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这意味着阴影军团的数量真的开始减少<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>起码从炮灰的角度来说<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不再是漫无边际了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>万里无云的晴天已经持续了很久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>阳光洒在大地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将积雪融化<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>明明是深冬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>九号却感受到了扑面而来的暖意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就像是春天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大圣<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>九号笑着道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我打小就喜欢您<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没想到有一天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也能和您并肩作战<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空一愣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>没想到九号会突然开口和自己说话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我还是喜欢叫您大圣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>虽然您已经成佛了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>希望您能一直潇洒下去<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>谢谢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空温和道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你也一样<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>九号点点头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>右手猛地拍在了机枪枪身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>金色的符咒霍然喷发出光芒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后飘浮在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>重机枪的枪身折叠旋转<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>所有零件都活了过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>拆分<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凝聚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>合成<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>重机枪眼花缭乱地变形<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终幻化为三把新的枪支悬在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>原本石台上的花纹平均分成三份<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>印刻在枪上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>流动着不同颜色的色泽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号抓住其中两柄硕大的左轮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在指尖绕了三绕<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>交叉双臂指向身体的两侧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他用脚尖挑起金色的步枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甩给孙悟空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>悟空伸手抓住步枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>疑惑地看向九号<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大圣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您知道热武器相比冷兵器<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最大的优势在哪吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>威力<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是便捷<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>借您的毫毛一用<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>九号道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>该开始清扫了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>九号深深地吸了一口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后吐出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>肾上腺素疯狂地分泌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随着血液运送到全身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他能听见自己的心跳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如撞钟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如战鼓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>激荡得血液都开始沸腾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他大步向前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>靴子在沁了雪水的泥土上留下深深的脚印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他越走越快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最终变成了极速奔行<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>血液冲击着他的大脑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他咆哮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手中的左轮赫然开火<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>金白色的光锥喷射而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轰碎了红色阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>九号双臂在身前画个半圆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>新月般地弹幕推进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>收割一片阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>枪就是拳的延伸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>九号完美地实现了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他屈膝弹射<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在地面留下浅坑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>猛地冲刺<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>双手在身前挥舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带出上百道残影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>每次挥舞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>总会伴随着阴影的溃散<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>火光冲天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>爆炸声不绝于耳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>九号的速度极快<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眨眼间就跑出去数百米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>清出了一条宽路<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空把毫毛撒在空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>无数猴子落地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>组成一支训练有素的军队<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>足足几千人的方阵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>给人视觉上极大的压迫感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空饶有兴趣地将步枪上膛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>瞄向远方的阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>开火<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>自由射击<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>该死<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华身上的衣服被撕裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>破烂不堪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣光都不再完美地凝聚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他护住头脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>祝融的烈焰灼烧着他的皮肤<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其烤得漆黑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>女娲又一次祭出山河社稷图<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>青光笼上了耶和华<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耶和华长啸一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>迎头而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的双手圣光爆发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>奋力插入长卷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>伴随着骨骼碎裂的声音<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>长卷被绞了个粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>蚩尤的掌心印上了耶和华的胸口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>将其拍得凹陷下去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他一口血喷出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脚下踉跄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>生生退了数十步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华站定<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>面目狰狞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>满是怨毒的神色<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>白色的火焰从脚底蹿上头顶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>烧毁了他的全部衣物<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>他们故意忘记<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从太古凭神的命有了天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>并从水而出藉水而成的地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>故此<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>当时的世界被水淹没就消灭了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华仰天大笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他双手高举过头顶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>圣光从云层投到他的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲的头皮都炸了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>死亡的气息席卷而来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>锁定了他的灵魂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他只觉得胸闷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>像被什么东西扼住了喉咙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这是真正可以灭世的能力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>耶和华能在地球站住脚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>掌控西方<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>与东方诸仙抗衡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一方面是东方神仙的逍遥性子使然<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>另一方面就在于他的底牌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>洪荒<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>伏羲甩动蛇尾<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>向前突进<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他捏了几个手印<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鳞片的缝隙中喷射出大量的蒸汽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同飙行的机车般撞入了光柱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>圣光洒在他的身上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不再有一贯温和的触感<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>反而似是强酸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把鳞片都烧得熔化<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>伏羲咬牙忍着剧痛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>怒吼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>重拳挥出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>五指捏住了伏羲的拳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力一握<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便把骨头捏了个粉碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>耶和华抬腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一脚把伏羲踢出百米开外<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他竟是靠着燃烧生命把自己的能力提升到了新的高度<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>就连战力最强的伏羲都不能坚持过一招<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>祝融几人对视<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>都感到一阵无力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>数千光弹仿佛流星般划过天空<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凶狠地在耶和华的后背炸开<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>射击声愈来愈近<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一支猴子组成的军队奔跑着开枪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>清扫着地面游荡的阴影<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>硝烟散尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>耶和华毫发无损地站在光柱中央<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘲讽地冲九号一笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他的脚下开始龟裂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大地疯狂地震动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>岩石崩塌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>火光从地壳的裂缝中透露出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>照亮了整个战场<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>震耳欲聋的水声响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轰隆的狂鸣充斥了众人的耳鼓<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>一线白色自远处平推过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是无垠的水墙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>天啊……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>伏羲微张了嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看着远处奔腾的浪潮<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他想起了万年以前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>耶和华初临的场景<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>二者如此的相似<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却又有着本质的区别<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>彼时仅仅是示威<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便使大陆沉没<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>而如今却是燃烧生命的同归于尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>离开地面<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>数百米的洪峰漫过了大地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吞噬了一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>除了耶和华和九号<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>所有人都腾空躲避<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>粼粼水波反射着阳光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在众人脸上映了光斑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号踏入了光柱之中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>催动洪荒消耗了耶和华大多数生命力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>之前年轻的面庞已然布满了皱纹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他矫健地挥拳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>挟带着蓬勃的圣光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号格挡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手臂蛇缠而上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他滑步扭身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只听嘎嘣一声脆响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>竟是生生将耶和华的手臂折断<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>怎么可能<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>耶和华的脸上露出了难以置信的神情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你怎么可能不受圣光影响<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>九号提膝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>凶狠地撞上了耶和华的侧腰<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>耶和华的生命随着洪荒的发展而流逝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>与九号相比<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>肉体上已经毫无分别<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他的肋骨穿透肌肉而出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>九号折断其中一根<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在手心变换方向后又插了回去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华的脸因为痛苦纠结成一团<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他抽着冷气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>又有什么用呢<span class=" fw-cl "><span>？</span></span>你们这群劣等物种<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我生命消亡之时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便是这星球毁灭之时<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>而你<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>应该为你的僭越感到抱歉<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>是吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>苍劲有力的声音如炸雷般响起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>鸿钧老祖一甩拂尘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在洪水中清出一座孤岛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>中央的光柱仍然通着天地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>却在威严之下黯淡无光<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>鸿钧老祖伸出手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻一弹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那光柱就支离破碎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>再也找不到曾存于世间的痕迹<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>耶和华瞪大了双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大脑一片空白<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>整个人如遭惊雷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>呆立不动<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>九号毫不留情地踢向耶和华的小腿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>左手用力<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>压得他跪在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我叫陈恪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第九号试验体<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>共和国中士<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>代号 c17<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>生而为人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我从不抱歉<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他把枪口顶在耶和华的太阳穴上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>还有<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>地球不需要上帝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>上帝死了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>阳光普照<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>45</p>
 <p>阳光透过窗子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>洒落到地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>酒吧里闹腾腾的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>充斥着人声的喧嚣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>乐队在台上演奏着轻快的歌曲<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>是 Ingrid Michaelson <em>的<span class="fw-op "><span>《</span></span>Everybod</em>y<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>》</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>吉他手微笑着弹琴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指拨动琴弦<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>鼓手把鼓槌抖出花来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脚下打着节拍<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>女主唱有着一头漆黑的长发<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她用一根发带将其束在脑后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>露出两个小巧精致的耳朵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>通透悦耳的歌声自她的喉间飘逸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直入心底<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>李中将<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>别来无恙<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺诧异地回头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>看到了青年嬉笑的脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>小陈啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>他笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>或许不应该再叫你小陈了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你现在可是英雄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>人类的救世主<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>李老<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>您还是别寒碜我了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我算什么救世主<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>陈恪脸红道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>没有您<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我或许早就死了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>更不要说什么屠神<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺苦笑着摇了摇头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>也不说话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>自顾自地摇晃着酒杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>使鲜红的葡萄酒液更充分地接触空气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他幽幽地叹了口气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>端起面前的酒杯啜饮一口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>眼帘低垂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>手指点着桌子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>好久才开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>你不恨我就好<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>未经你同意就把你推上前线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我其实一直都很后悔<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>陈恪没想到自己的事居然成了李平恺心中的负担<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他整理了神情<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正色望着面前的老人<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>缓缓开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>不是的<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>李平恺抬头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>盯着陈恪的眼睛<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>不是的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>李中将<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>陈恪毫无躲闪<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>语气无比真挚<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我可以用我所拥有的东西去换点什么<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>懦弱不再使我向现实下跪求饶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>这些就是我在您这里所得到的东西<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span>尊严和荣耀<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>您不知道这些对我有多么重要<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我失去了一切<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>它们是我生存的唯一理由<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>所以<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>，</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>陈恪从桌边站起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>深深地对李平恺鞠了一躬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>谢谢您<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>猴哥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就连师父都在这聊天<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你揪俺俩出来干啥<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>猪八戒慢悠悠跟在孙悟空屁股后面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>满腹的抱怨<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空被吵得烦了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转身一探<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一把掐住猪八戒的大耳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力把他拽到自己面前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>恶狠狠道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>呆子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一天天哪来那么多废话<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你看沙师弟<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从来都不多嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你就不能学习学习<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>猪八戒被掐得疼了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>急忙告饶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>心里却是骂起了弼马温<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>迫于无奈<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>只能是脚下踢着石子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不情不愿地小跑几步<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空唤出了筋斗云<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>招呼二人上去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>刚刚站稳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>便猛地加速<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>筋斗云载着三人掠过数千千米<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>初春的大地已经泛起了油油的绿<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>从高空看着地面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>根本无法与几个月前的战争联系在一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空恶趣味地冲入返乡的鸟群<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻轻敲了敲大雁的头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>鸟被惊得哀鸣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>粪便喷射出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>甩了猪八戒一头一脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>弼马温<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哈哈哈哈哈哈<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>悟空爽朗大笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>伸开双臂<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>拥抱着自由的风<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>几分钟后<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>三人降落在一处干涸的沟渠边上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>入目处便是龟裂的大地<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>显然水源已经枯竭了很久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大师兄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这儿是哪<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>沙悟净开口询问<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空在唇间竖起一根手指<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>神秘地从怀中掏出一个白玉瓶子<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>柳枝在瓶口插着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>青翠得惹人怜爱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他拈起柳枝<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>把上面沾着的露水洒在地上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>泥土以肉眼可见的速度湿润起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>这是<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>猪八戒瞪大了双眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>猴哥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你居然把菩萨的东西偷来了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>悟空扭头怒视<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>吓得八戒急忙捂住了嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他轻哼一声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>皱起了眉头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>不满道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>怎么这么慢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>孙悟空把玉净在耳边摇了摇<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>嘴角扬起了坏笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>直接倒转过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>清澈的水瞬间充满了河流<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>有金色的鲤鱼跃出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>溅起一片水花<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>绿色以河流为起点向外蔓延<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>转眼就铺满了整面山坡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>水花激荡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>滚滚而去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在不远处的山崖边缘向下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>飞漱清扬<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>桃花骨朵从枯树的枝干上钻了出来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>又倏忽绽放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>一团粉红随风摇曳<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>刹那间落英纷飞<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>惊起一群不知何时出现的彩蝶<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>流苏般的阳光穿过白云<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>透过树荫<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>在瀑布旁挥笔画下一道虹桥<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>正好圈住了那隐藏其后的洞府<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>三人看得呆了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>许久<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>悟空才颤抖着开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>花果山<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>水帘洞<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>奎托斯撑着下巴看着枕边的人痴笑<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他伸手出去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>轻抚那如凝脂一般的脸颊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>睫毛微颤轻启<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>水沁的眸子盯着奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>弯成一弦初月<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你好美……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯喃喃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜双颊泛起了些许酡红<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>偏头避开了奎托斯的视线<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>蠢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>她道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后一把推开奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>裹着毯子站了起来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我想过了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>平凡人的生活太无趣了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>所以从今天起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我还是女神<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>猪猡<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你可以滚了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>啊<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>奎托斯没反应过来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我说你可以滚了<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>奎托斯蒙了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>慌忙站起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>双手不知道放在哪里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>四处挥了几下<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>最后贴到腿边<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>摆出一副小学生立正的姿势<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>雅典娜看着傻眼的奎托斯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>板不住脸<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>扑哧一下笑出了声<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你们两个到底谁放出来的电压比较高<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>杨戬靠在吧台<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>歪着头问道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>大概是他<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>雷震子翻了个白眼<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>冲着索尔努努嘴<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>索尔听了心情舒爽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>锤子往身边一放<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>露出了满口白牙<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>咧嘴笑道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>那是<span class=" fw-cl "><span>！</span></span>我当初奉命去华夏<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>第一个遇到的就是雷兄<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>你说是不是够巧合的<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>两个同样用电的人居然就对上了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>要说雷兄也是一把好手<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>可惜遇上了我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>哈哈哈……呃……你们别这么看着我……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒斜眼瞅着索尔<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>乾坤圈在手指上绕来绕去<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他侧了侧头<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>颈椎发出了嘎嘣的声响<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>其实我觉得<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>还是雷兄更厉害<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>索尔收起笑容<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>严肃地说道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>酒吧里又重新充满了快活的空气<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哪吒笑着抬起酒杯<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>站起身来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>我提议<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>就算是为了仍然活着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大家也应该干一杯<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>几人都把酒杯满上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>用力地碰在了一起<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>然后一饮而尽<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>酒精顺着喉咙流入胃里<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>随着血液散发到全身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>暖气由内向外扑出<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>带着陈酿的醇香<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>索尔红光满面<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把杯子拍在桌上<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大声叫嚷<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>光喝酒嘴里太空了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>听说这里有样招牌菜<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大家要不要尝尝<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>众人来了兴趣<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>纷纷询问菜名<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>索尔很享受这种被包围的感觉<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>他把手心向下压了压<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>待人群安静下来才开口道<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>狗肉炖藕<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>！</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>你找碴是吧<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span>哪吒掀桌<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>哎<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你咋打人呢<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>我<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>我要还手了啊<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>你别以为我不敢……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>别打了大哥……<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
 <p>女主唱伸手扯下了发带<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>抛到空中<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>长发散落下来<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>如同漆色的瀑布<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>她嘴角带着笑意<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>那是对生活的热忱<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>10 年了<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>10 年前的她<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>大概才刚上大学<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>陈恪看着眼前的姑娘<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>这么想着<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>脑海里浮现出种种回忆<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>阳光更多地射入酒吧<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>安抚着每一个人的心灵<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>您很面熟<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>。</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>陈恪起身<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>走到台前<span class=" fw-cl "><span>。</span></span>他从西装的口袋里摸出褶皱不堪的泛黄相片晃了晃<span class=" fw-cl "><span>，</span></span>温柔地开口<span class=" fw-cl "><span>：</span></span><span class="fw-op fw--collapsed"><span>「</span></span>能请您跳支舞吗<span class=" fw-cl fw--collapsed"><span>？</span></span><span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span class="fw-op "><span>「</span></span>Everybody, everybody wants to love.</p>
 <p>Everybody, everybody wants to be loved.</p>
 <p>Oh, oh, oh, oh, oh, oh.</p>
 <p>oh everybody knows the love,</p>
 <p>everybody holds the love.</p>
 <p>everybody folds for love.</p>
 <p>everybody feels with love, everybody steals with love.</p>
 <p>everybody heals with love.</p>
 <p>oh oh oh oh,just let the love love love begin.<span class=" fw-cl "><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>□ 温酒</p>
